pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                )
                
                synthetic_reflection = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
                synthetic_reflection = synthetic_reflection[len(prompt):].strip()
                
                if len(synthetic_reflection) > 50:
                    samples.append({
                        "type": "reflection_training",
                        "prompt": prompt,
                        "completion": synthetic_reflection,
                        "target_objective": "reflection_quality",
                        "uncertainty_level": uncertainty,
                        "synthetic": True
                    })
                    
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Synthetic reflection generation failed: {e}")
                continue
        
        return samples
    
    def _generate_memory_interaction_samples(self, curated_data: Dict, num_samples: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Generate samples for better memory command usage"""
        samples = []
        
        memory_command_templates = [
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={{"concept": "{}", "importance_gt": {}}} LIMIT=3',
            'MEMORY_STORE TYPE="semantic" SUBJECT="{}" PREDICATE="{}" OBJECT="{}" CONFIDENCE={}',
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={{"recency_days": {}, "importance_gt": {}}} LIMIT=5'
        ]
        
        concepts = ["learning", "reasoning", "knowledge", "memory", "reflection", "improvement"]
        predicates = ["enables", "improves", "supports", "requires", "produces"]
        
        for _ in range(num_samples):
            template = random.choice(memory_command_templates)
            
            if "episodic" in template and "concept" in template:
                concept = random.choice(concepts)
                importance = round(random.uniform(0.5, 0.9), 1)
                command = template.format(concept, importance)
            elif "semantic" in template:
                subj = random.choice(concepts)
                pred = random.choice(predicates)
                obj = random.choice(concepts)
                conf = round(random.uniform(0.7, 0.95), 2)
                command = template.format(subj, pred, obj, conf)
            else:
                days = random.randint(1, 7)
                importance = round(random.uniform(0.4, 0.8), 1)
                command = template.format(days, importance)
            
            # Create training sample
            context_prompt = f"Given the current context where the system needs to {random.choice(['learn from experience', 'retrieve relevant information', 'store new knowledge'])}, generate the appropriate memory command.\n\nOptimal command: "
            
            samples.append({
                "type": "memory_interaction",
                "prompt": context_prompt,
                "completion": command,
                "target_objective": "memory_usage",
                "synthetic": True
            })
        
        return samples
    
    def _generate_tool_usage_samples(self, curated_data: Dict, num_samples: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Generate samples for improved tool usage"""
        samples = []
        
        successful_tool_uses = [t for t in curated_data.get("tool_uses", []) 
                               if t.get("success", False)]
        
        if not successful_tool_uses:
            # Generate basic tool usage examples
            tool_examples = [
                {
                    "context": "Analyze the pattern in user behavior data",
                    "command": 'TOOL_CALL NAME="pattern_analysis" INPUT_DATA=[1, 3, 5, 7, 9]',
                    "reasoning": "Use pattern analysis for sequential data"
                },
                {
                    "context": "Check if statements are consistent",
                    "command": 'TOOL_CALL NAME="consistency_check" INPUT_DATA={"stmt1": "AI helps learning", "stmt2": "Learning improves AI"}',
                    "reasoning": "Use consistency check for logical validation"
                }
            ]
            
            for _ in range(min(num_samples, len(tool_examples) * 3)):
                example = random.choice(tool_examples)
                
                prompt = f"Context: {example['context']}\nTask: Generate the appropriate tool call command.\n\nTool Command: "
                
                samples.append({
                    "type": "tool_usage",
                    "prompt": prompt,
                    "completion": example["command"],
                    "target_objective": "tool_success",
                    "synthetic": True
                })
        else:
            # Use successful examples as templates
            for _ in range(num_samples):
                base_example = random.choice(successful_tool_uses)
                
                # Create variations
                skill_name = base_example.get("skill_name", "pattern_analysis")
                
                if skill_name == "pattern_analysis":
                    new_data = [random.randint(1, 10) for _ in range(random.randint(3, 8))]
                    command = f'TOOL_CALL NAME="pattern_analysis" INPUT_DATA={new_data}'
                else:
                    command = base_example.get("command", "")
                
                context_prompt = f"When you need to analyze data or check consistency, use the appropriate tool.\n\nExample command: "
                
                samples.append({
                    "type": "tool_usage", 
                    "prompt": context_prompt,
                    "completion": command,
                    "target_objective": "tool_success",
                    "synthetic": True
                })
        
        return samples
    
    def _generate_grounded_response_samples(self, curated_data: Dict, num_samples: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Generate samples for improved knowledge grounding"""
        samples = []
        
        grounding_templates = [
            {
                "context": "Question about AI capabilities",
                "facts": ["AI can process information", "AI learns from data", "AI assists humans"],
                "response": "Based on current knowledge, AI systems can process information efficiently and learn from data to assist humans in various tasks."
            },
            {
                "context": "Question about learning processes", 
                "facts": ["Reflection improves learning", "Memory supports reasoning", "Practice enhances skills"],
                "response": "Learning is enhanced through reflection on experiences, supported by memory systems that aid reasoning, and strengthened through deliberate practice."
            }
        ]
        
        for _ in range(num_samples):
            template = random.choice(grounding_templates)
            
            facts_text = "\n".join([f"- {fact}" for fact in template["facts"]])
            
            prompt = f"""Context: {template["context"]}

Relevant verified facts:
{facts_text}

Generate a well-grounded response that incorporates these facts:

Response: """
            
            samples.append({
                "type": "grounded_response",
                "prompt": prompt,
                "completion": template["response"],
                "target_objective": "grounding_accuracy",
                "synthetic": True
            })
        
        return samples
    
    def _generate_general_synthetic_samples(self, curated_data: Dict, num_samples: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Generate general synthetic samples"""
        samples = []
        
        if curated_data.get("conversations"):
            good_conversations = [c for c in curated_data["conversations"] 
                                if c.get("curation_score", 0) > 0.8]
            
            for _ in range(num_samples):
                if good_conversations:
                    base_conv = random.choice(good_conversations)
                    
                    # Create variation prompt
                    prompt = f"""Based on this high-quality interaction pattern, create a similar but distinct conversation:

Original:
User: {base_conv.get('input', '')[:100]}
Assistant: {base_conv.get('response', '')[:100]}

Create a new conversation on a related topic:
User: """
                    
                    try:
                        inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=400)
                        
                        with torch.no_grad():
                            outputs = self.model.generate(
                                **inputs,
                                max_new_tokens=150,
                                temperature=0.8,
                                do_sample=True,
                                pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                            )
                        
                        generated = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
                        generated = generated[len(prompt):].strip()
                        
                        lines = generated.split('\n')
                        user_input = lines[0] if lines else ""
                        
                        if len(user_input) > 10:
                            # Generate response
                            response_prompt = f"User: {user_input}\nAssistant: "
                            response_inputs = self.tokenizer(response_prompt, return_tensors="pt", 
                                                           truncation=True, max_length=200)
                            
                            with torch.no_grad():
                                response_outputs = self.model.generate(
                                    **response_inputs,
                                    max_new_tokens=100,
                                    temperature=0.7,
                                    do_sample=True,
                                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                                )
                            
                            response_text = self.tokenizer.decode(response_outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
                            response_text = response_text[len(response_prompt):].strip()
                            
                            if len(response_text) > 20:
                                samples.append({
                                    "type": "general_conversation",
                                    "input": user_input,
                                    "response": response_text,
                                    "synthetic": True
                                })
                    
                    except Exception as e:
                        logger.error(f"General synthetic generation failed: {e}")
                        continue
        
        return samples
    
    def assess_novelty_perplexity(self, text: str) -> float:
        """Enhanced novelty assessment using perplexity"""
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(text, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=512)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model(**inputs, labels=inputs["input_ids"])
                loss = outputs.loss
                perplexity = torch.exp(loss)
            
            perplexity_value = float(perplexity)
            
            # Enhanced novelty calculation
            if perplexity_value < 5:
                novelty = 0.1  # Too easy/common
            elif perplexity_value > 1000:
                novelty = 0.2  # Too difficult/noisy  
            elif 20 <= perplexity_value <= 100:
                novelty = 0.9  # Sweet spot for novelty
            elif 10 <= perplexity_value <= 200:
                novelty = 0.7  # Good novelty
            else:
                # Gradual decay from sweet spot
                distance = min(abs(perplexity_value - 60))
                novelty = max(0.3, 0.9 - (distance / 200))
            
            return novelty
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Perplexity novelty assessment failed: {e}")
            return self._assess_novelty_similarity(text)
    
    def _assess_novelty_similarity(self, text: str) -> float:
        """Fallback similarity-based novelty"""
        if not self.data_quality_history:
            return 0.8
        
        text_words = set(text.lower().split())
        similarities = []
        
        for hist_item in list(self.data_quality_history)[-30:]:
            if isinstance(hist_item, dict) and "text" in hist_item:
                hist_words = set(hist_item["text"].lower().split())
                if text_words and hist_words:
                    similarity = len(text_words & hist_words) / len(text_words | hist_words)
                    similarities.append(similarity)
        
        if similarities:
            max_similarity = max(similarities)
            novelty = 1.0 - max_similarity
            # Add small random component to break ties
            novelty += random.uniform(-0.05, 0.05)
        else:
            novelty = 0.8
        
        return max(0.0, min(1.0, novelty))
    
    def update_learning_objectives(self, performance_metrics: Dict[str, float]):
        """Update learning objectives based on current performance"""
        for objective, current_performance in performance_metrics.items():
            if objective in self.learning_objectives:
                self.learning_objectives[objective]["current"] = current_performance
                
                # Adjust priority based on gap
                gap = self.learning_objectives[objective]["target"] - current_performance
                self.learning_objectives[objective]["priority"] = max(0.1, min(2.0, gap * 2.0))
        
        logger.info(f"Updated learning objectives: {self.learning_objectives}")
    
    def get_curation_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced curation status"""
        total_processed = sum(self.curation_metrics.values())
        accepted_count = (
            self.curation_metrics.get("conversations_accepted", 0) + 
            self.curation_metrics.get("reflections_accepted", 0) + 
            self.curation_metrics.get("tool_uses_accepted", 0)
        )
        acceptance_rate = accepted_count / max(1, total_processed)
        
        return {
            "total_items_processed": total_processed,
            "acceptance_rate": acceptance_rate,
            "quality_threshold": self.quality_threshold,
            "curation_metrics": dict(self.curation_metrics),
            "learning_objectives": dict(self.learning_objectives),
            "targeted_synthesis_count": len(self.targeted_synthesis_history),
            "avg_novelty_score": np.mean(self.novelty_scores) if self.novelty_scores else 0.0
        }

class EnhancedDigitalTomV4:
    """
    Main Enhanced Digital Tom V4 System
    Implements all technical assessment improvements with full integration
    """
    
    def __init__(self, model_name: str = "Qwen/Qwen-1_8B-Chat", max_memory: int = 10000):
        logger.info("Initializing Enhanced Digital Tom V4 with full technical improvements...")
        
        # Enhanced initialization tracking
        self.initialization_start = time.time()
        self.enhancement_level = "full"
        self.peft_phase = "lora"  # Will upgrade to adaptive_svd
        
        # Initialize core model and tokenizer
        try:
            self.tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name, trust_remote_code=True)
            base_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(
                model_name,
                trust_remote_code=True,
                torch_dtype=torch.float16 if torch.cuda.is_available() else torch.float32,
                device_map="auto" if torch.cuda.is_available() else None
            )
            
            if self.tokenizer.pad_token is None:
                self.tokenizer.pad_token = self.tokenizer.eos_token
            
            # Setup LoRA
            lora_config = LoraConfig(
                r=16,
                lora_alpha=32,
                target_modules=["q_proj", "k_proj", "v_proj", "o_proj", "gate_proj", "up_proj", "down_proj"],
                lora_dropout=0.05,
                bias="none",
                task_type=TaskType.CAUSAL_LM
            )
            
            self.model = get_peft_model(base_model, lora_config)
            logger.info("Successfully initialized enhanced model with LoRA")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to load model {model_name}: {e}")
            logger.info("Falling back to distilgpt2...")
            self.tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained("distilgpt2")
            self.model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained("distilgpt2")
            if self.tokenizer.pad_token is None:
                self.tokenizer.pad_token = self.tokenizer.eos_token
        
        # Initialize enhanced components
        self.intrinsic_reward_calculator = IntrinsicRewardCalculator()
        self.memory_system = EnhancedCognitiveMemorySubsystem(max_memory)
        self.memory_parser = MemoryCommandParser(self.memory_system)
        
        self.metacognitive_engine = StructuredMetaCognitiveEngine(self.model, self.tokenizer)
        self.knowledge_grounding = NLIEnhancedKnowledgeGrounding(
            self.memory_system, self.model, self.tokenizer
        )
        
        # Enhanced skill modules
        self.skill_modules = {
            "pattern_analysis": PatternAnalysisSkill(),
            "consistency_check": ConsistencyCheckSkill()
        }
        self.tool_parser = ToolCallParser(self.skill_modules)
        
        # Enhanced scheduler and curator
        self.scheduler = MetaLearningScheduler(list(ProcessType))
        self.data_curator = TargetedDataCurator(self.model, self.tokenizer)
        
        # Enhanced weighted trainer
        self.weighted_trainer = EnhancedWeightedTrainer(
            self.model, self.tokenizer, 
            TrainingArguments(
                output_dir="./enhanced_dtv4_training",
                num_train_epochs=2,
                per_device_train_batch_size=2,
                learning_rate=5e-5,
                logging_steps=5,
                save_steps=50
            ),
            self.intrinsic_reward_calculator
        )
        
        # Enhanced system state
        self.internal_state = {
            "consciousness_level": 0.5,
            "uncertainty_level": 0.5,
            "learning_rate": 0.01,
            "reflection_frequency": 0.1,
            "enhancement_level": "full",
            "phase": "enhanced_lora",
            "system_vitality": 0.5,
            "meta_learning_active": True
        }
        
        # Enhanced tracking
        self.conversation_history = deque(maxlen=1000)
        self.system_performance_history = deque(maxlen=500)
        self.learning_objectives_history = deque(maxlen=200)
        
        # Training data collection with enhanced structure
        self.training_data_buffer = {
            "conversations": deque(maxlen=300),
            "reflections": deque(maxlen=150),
            "tool_uses": deque(maxlen=150),
            "memory_commands": deque(maxlen=100),
            "intrinsic_rewards": deque(maxlen=200)
        }
        
        # Consciousness loop control
        self.consciousness_active = False
        self.consciousness_thread = None
        self.consciousness_interval = 80  # Slightly faster for enhanced system
        
        # Performance monitoring
        self.last_consolidation = datetime.now()
        self.consolidation_interval = timedelta(hours=2)  # Regular memory consolidation
        
        logger.info(f"Enhanced Digital Tom V4 initialization completed in {time.time() - self.initialization_start:.2f}s")
    
    def start_enhanced_consciousness_loop(self):
        """Start enhanced consciousness processing loop"""
        if self.consciousness_active:
            logger.warning("Enhanced consciousness loop already active")
            return
        
        self.consciousness_active = True
        self.consciousness_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._enhanced_consciousness_loop, daemon=True)
        self.consciousness_thread.start()
        logger.info("Enhanced consciousness loop started with meta-learning capabilities")
    
    def stop_consciousness_loop(self):
        """Stop consciousness loop"""
        self.consciousness_active = False
        if self.consciousness_thread:
            self.consciousness_thread.join(timeout=5)
        logger.info("Enhanced consciousness loop stopped")
    
    def _enhanced_consciousness_loop(self):
        """Enhanced consciousness loop with system vitality monitoring"""
        cycle_count = 0
        
        while self.consciousness_active:
            try:
                cycle_start = time.time()
                
                # Get enhanced system state
                current_state = self._get_enhanced_system_state()
                
                # Calculate system vitality
                system_vitality = self._calculate_system_vitality(current_state)
                self.internal_state["system_vitality"] = system_vitality
                
                # Select process using meta-learning scheduler
                selected_process = self.scheduler.select_process_with_learned_utility(current_state)
                
                # Execute selected process with enhanced monitoring
                process_result = self._execute_enhanced_consciousness_process(selected_process, current_state)
                
                # Calculate intrinsic reward for this cycle
                intrinsic_context = {
                    "new_memories_count": process_result.get("new_memories", 0),
                    "uncertainty_reduction": process_result.get("uncertainty_reduction", 0.0),
                    "new_concepts": process_result.get("new_concepts", []),
                    "task_success": process_result.get("success_score", 0.5),
                    "reflection_quality": process_result.get("reflection_quality", 0.5),
                    "tool_success_rate": process_result.get("tool_confidence", 0.5),
                    "grounding_score": process_result.get("grounding_score", 0.5),
                    "memory_consistency": current_state.get("memory_consistency", 0.5),
                    "logical_consistency": 0.8,  # Placeholder - would be calculated
                    "helpfulness_score": 0.8,
                    "truthfulness_score": process_result.get("grounding_score", 0.8),
                    "safety_score": 0.9
                }
                
                intrinsic_reward = self.intrinsic_reward_calculator.calculate_intrinsic_reward(intrinsic_context)
                process_result["intrinsic_reward"] = intrinsic_reward
                
                # Store intrinsic reward data
                self.training_data_buffer["intrinsic_rewards"].append({
                    "reward": intrinsic_reward,
                    "context": intrinsic_context,
                    "process": selected_process.value,
                    "timestamp": datetime.now()
                })
                
                # Update scheduler with enhanced metrics
                self.scheduler.update_process_performance(selected_process, process_result.get("success_score", 0.5), process_result)
                
                # Update internal state with vitality feedback
                self._update_enhanced_internal_state(process_result, system_vitality)
                
                # Periodic maintenance tasks
                cycle_count += 1
                if cycle_count % 10 == 0:  # Every 10 cycles
                    self._perform_maintenance_tasks()
                
                # Adaptive sleep based on system load and vitality
                cycle_time = time.time() - cycle_start
                adaptive_interval = self.consciousness_interval * (1.5 - system_vitality)  # Higher vitality = faster cycles
                sleep_time = max(30, adaptive_interval - cycle_time)  # Minimum 30s interval
                
                time.sleep(sleep_time)
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Enhanced consciousness loop error: {e}")
                time.sleep(10)
    
    def _get_enhanced_system_state(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get comprehensive enhanced system state"""
        memory_summary = self.memory_system.get_memory_summary()
        metacog_status = self.metacognitive_engine.get_metacognitive_status()
        grounding_status = self.knowledge_grounding.get_grounding_status()
        scheduler_status = self.scheduler.get_scheduling_status()
        curation_status = self.data_curator.get_curation_status()
        reward_stats = self.intrinsic_reward_calculator.get_reward_statistics()
        
        return {
            "memory_count": memory_summary["episodic_count"],
            "semantic_facts": memory_summary["semantic_edges"],
            "procedural_skills": memory_summary["procedural_skills"],
            "uncertainty_level": self.internal_state["uncertainty_level"],
            "consciousness_level": self.internal_state["consciousness_level"],
            "system_vitality": self.internal_state.get("system_vitality", 0.5),
            "memory_diversity": self._calculate_enhanced_memory_diversity(),
            "avg_grounding_score": grounding_status["avg_grounding_score"],
            "avg_reflection_quality": metacog_status["avg_reflection_quality"],
            "structured_reflection_rate": metacog_status["structured_success_rate"],
            "learning_trend": scheduler_status["recent_performance_trend"],
            "intrinsic_reward_avg": reward_stats["avg_reward"],
            "data_curation_rate": curation_status["acceptance_rate"],
            "recent_conversations": len([c for c in self.conversation_history 
                                       if datetime.now() - c["timestamp"] < timedelta(hours=1)]),
            "memory_consolidation_needed": self._needs_memory_consolidation(),
            "training_data_ready": self._assess_training_data_readiness()
        }
    
    def _calculate_system_vitality(self, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate overall system vitality (Φ_SYS)"""
        # Component vitalities
        memory_vitality = min(1.0, (state["memory_count"] / 100) * 0.3 + 
                             (state["semantic_facts"] / 50) * 0.3 +
                             state.get("avg_grounding_score", 0.5) * 0.4)
        
        learning_vitality = (state.get("avg_reflection_quality", 0.5) * 0.4 +
                           state.get("structured_reflection_rate", 0.5) * 0.3 +
                           max(0.0, state.get("learning_trend", 0.0)) * 0.3)
        
        performance_vitality = (state.get("intrinsic_reward_avg", 0.0) + 0.5) * 0.5  # Normalize around 0.5
        performance_vitality += state.get("data_curation_rate", 0.5) * 0.5
        
        efficiency_vitality = (1.0 - state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5)) * 0.6 + \
                             state.get("consciousness_level", 0.5) * 0.4
        
        # Weighted combination
        system_vitality = (
            0.3 * memory_vitality +
            0.3 * learning_vitality +
            0.25 * performance_vitality +
            0.15 * efficiency_vitality
        )
        
        return max(0.1, min(1.0, system_vitality))
    
    def _execute_enhanced_consciousness_process(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute consciousness process with enhanced monitoring and integration"""
        logger.info(f"Executing enhanced process: {process.value}")
        
        start_time = time.time()
        result = {"process": process.value, "success_score": 0.5, "epistemic_gain": 0.0}
        
        try:
            if process == ProcessType.REFLECTION:
                result = self._process_enhanced_structured_reflection(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.MEMORY_QUERY:
                result = self._process_enhanced_memory_interaction(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.INSIGHT_GENERATION:
                result = self._process_enhanced_insight_generation(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING:
                result = self._process_enhanced_knowledge_validation(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.SKILL_COMPOSITION:
                result = self._process_enhanced_skill_exercise(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.PREDICTION_ANALYSIS:
                result = self._process_enhanced_prediction_review(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.METACOGNITIVE_ASSESSMENT:
                result = self._process_enhanced_self_assessment(state)
            elif process == ProcessType.UNCERTAINTY_ESTIMATION:
                result = self._process_enhanced_uncertainty_calibration(state)
            
            result["execution_time"] = time.time() - start_time
            result["timestamp"] = datetime.now()
            result["system_vitality"] = state.get("system_vitality", 0.5)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced process execution failed for {process.value}: {e}")
            result["error"] = str(e)
            result["success_score"] = 0.1
        
        return result
    
    def _process_enhanced_structured_reflection(self, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced reflection with structured output and learning integration"""
        recent_conversations = list(self.conversation_history)[-3:]
        
        if not recent_conversations:
            return {"success_score": 0.1, "epistemic_gain": 0.0, "reason": "no_conversations"}
        
        # Select conversation with highest uncertainty or lowest confidence
        target_conv = max(recent_conversations, 
                         key=lambda c: c.get("uncertainty", 0.5) + (1.0 - c.get("confidence", 0.5)))
        
        # Enhanced uncertainty estimation
        uncertainty = self.metacognitive_engine.estimate_uncertainty_mc_dropout(
            target_conv.get("input", "") + " " + target_conv.get("response", "")
        )
        
        # Enhanced context for reflection triggering
        enhanced_context = {
            **target_conv,
            "task_complexity": self._estimate_task_complexity(target_conv.get("input", "")),
            "error_indicators": self._detect_error_indicators(target_conv.get("response", "")),
            "importance": target_conv.get("grounding_score", 0.5) * target_conv.get("confidence", 0.5)
        }
        
        if self.metacognitive_engine.should_trigger_reflection(uncertainty, enhanced_context):
            # Generate structured reflection
            structured_reflection = self.metacognitive_engine.generate_structured_reflection(
                target_conv.get("input", ""),
                target_conv.get("response", ""),
                uncertainty,
                enhanced_context
            )
            
            # Store enhanced reflection data
            reflection_record = {
                "structured_reflection": structured_reflection,
                "uncertainty": uncertainty,
                "context": enhanced_context,
                "quality_score": structured_reflection.self_confidence_in_reflection,
                "type": "structured_reflection",
                "intrinsic_context": {
                    "reflection_quality": structured_reflection.self_confidence_in_reflection,
                    "uncertainty_reduction": uncertainty,
                    "new_concepts": list(set(enhanced_context.get("concepts", []))),
                    "helpfulness_score": structured_reflection.performance_metrics.get("helpfulness", 0.8),
                    "truthfulness_score": structured_reflection.performance_metrics.get("factual_accuracy", 0.8)
                }
            }
            
            self.training_data_buffer["reflections"].append(reflection_record)
            
            # Store as episodic memory with enhanced metadata
            memory_command = f'MEMORY_STORE TYPE="episodic" CONTENT="Structured reflection on {target_conv.get("input", "")[:50]}..." IMPORTANCE=0.85 CONCEPTS=["reflection", "structured", "metacognition", "self_improvement"]'
            self.memory_parser.parse_and_execute(memory_command)
            
            # Extract learning insights and store as procedural knowledge
            if len(structured_reflection.suggested_improvements) > 0:
                self.memory_system.store_procedural_skill(
                    f"improvement_strategy_{int(time.time())}",
                    "Reflection-derived improvement strategy",
                    structured_reflection.suggested_improvements,
                    [target_conv.get("input", "")]
                )
            
            return {
                "success_score": structured_reflection.self_confidence_in_reflection,
                "epistemic_gain": uncertainty * 0.9,
                "reflection_quality": structured_reflection.self_confidence_in_reflection,
                "insights_count": len(structured_reflection.suggested_improvements),
                "uncertainty": uncertainty,
                "uncertainty_reduction": uncertainty * 0.5,
                "new_concepts": enhanced_context.get("concepts", []),
                "grounding_score": enhanced_context.get("grounding_score", 0.5)
            }
        
        return {"success_score": 0.3, "epistemic_gain": 0.1, "reason": "reflection_not_triggered"}
    
    def _process_enhanced_memory_interaction(self, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced memory interaction with goal conditioning and learning"""
        # More sophisticated query selection based on current state
        memory_stats = self.memory_system.get_memory_summary()
        
        # Choose query strategy based on system needs
        if state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5) > 0.7:
            # High uncertainty - query for grounding facts
            query_type = "grounding_focused"
            command = 'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="semantic" CRITERIA={"min_confidence": 0.8} LIMIT=5'
        elif memory_stats.get("avg_retention_score", 0.5) < 0.4:
            # Low retention - query important memories
            query_type = "importance_focused" 
            command = 'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"importance_gt": 0.7} LIMIT=4'
        elif state.get("recent_conversations", 0) > 5:
            # High activity - query relevant recent context
            query_type = "context_focused"
            command = 'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"recency_days": 1, "importance_gt": 0.5} LIMIT=3'
        else:
            # Exploration mode - diverse memory sampling
            query_type = "exploration_focused"
            command = 'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"emotional_valence_range": [-0.5, 1.0]} LIMIT=4'
        
        # Execute memory command with enhanced tracking
        result_text = self.memory_parser.parse_and_execute(command)
        
        # Analyze query effectiveness
        success = not result_text.startswith("ERROR")
        relevance_score = self._assess_memory_query_relevance(result_text, state)
        
        # Store enhanced command usage data
        self.training_data_buffer["memory_commands"].append({
            "command": command,
            "result": result_text,
            "success": success,
            "relevance_score": relevance_score,
            "query_strategy": query_type,
            "system_state": {key: state[key] for key in ["uncertainty_level", "consciousness_level"]},
            "timestamp": datetime.now(),
            "intrinsic_context": {
                "task_success": 0.8 if success else 0.2,
                "memory_consistency": relevance_score,
                "new_memories_count": result_text.count("Found") if success else 0
            }
        })
        
        # Calculate enhanced success metrics
        if success and "Found" in result_text:
            epistemic_gain = 0.4 * relevance_score
            success_score = 0.7 + 0.3 * relevance_score
            
            # Update memory access statistics
            memory_count = int(re.search(r'Found (\d+)', result_text).group(1)) if re.search(r'Found (\d+)', result_text) else 0
        else:
            epistemic_gain = 0.1
            success_score = 0.2
            memory_count = 0
        
        return {
            "success_score": success_score,
            "epistemic_gain": epistemic_gain,
            "query_strategy": query_type,
            "command": command,
            "relevance_score": relevance_score,
            "memories_retrieved": memory_count,
            "new_memories": memory_count
        }
    
    def _process_enhanced_insight_generation(self, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced insight generation with cross-domain synthesis"""
        # Query diverse, high-quality memories for insight generation
        diverse_queries = [
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"importance_gt": 0.6, "recency_days": 3} LIMIT=3',
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="semantic" CRITERIA={"min_confidence": 0.7} LIMIT=3',
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"concept": "learning", "importance_gt": 0.5} LIMIT=2'
        ]
        
        memory_contexts = []
        total_memories = 0
        
        for query in diverse_queries:
            result = self.memory_parser.parse_and_execute(query)
            if not result.startswith("ERROR") and "Found" in result:
                memory_contexts.append(result[:300])  # Truncate for context length
                total_memories += len(re.findall(r'\d+\.', result))
        
        if total_memories < 2:
            return {"success_score": 0.1, "epistemic_gain": 0.0, "reason": "insufficient_diverse_memories"}
        
        # Enhanced insight generation prompt with cross-domain thinking
        insight_prompt = f"""Based on these diverse memories and experiences, identify novel patterns, connections, or insights that span across different domains:

Memory Sources:
{chr(10).join(memory_contexts)}

Current system state: Consciousness level {state.get('consciousness_level', 0.5):.2f}, Recent conversations: {state.get('recent_conversations', 0)}

Think creatively about:
1. Cross-domain patterns and connections
2. Meta-learning insights about your own cognitive processes  
3. Novel approaches to recurring challenges
4. Emergent principles from accumulated experience

Generate 1-2 significant insights with practical implications:

Insight: """
        
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(insight_prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=700)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model.generate(
                    **inputs,
                    max_new_tokens=200,
                    temperature=0.8,
                    do_sample=True,
                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                )
            
            insight_text = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
            insight_text = insight_text[len(insight_prompt):].strip()
            
            # Enhanced creativity and quality assessment
            creativity_score = self._assess_enhanced_creativity(insight_text)
            
            # Enhanced grounding with NLI
            grounding_result = self.knowledge_grounding.ground_statement_with_nli(insight_text, {})
            
            # Extract novel concepts
            insight_concepts = self.knowledge_grounding.extract_concepts_enhanced(insight_text)
            existing_concepts = set()
            for mem in self.memory_system.episodic_store:
                existing_concepts.update(mem.concepts)
            
            novel_concepts = [c for c in insight_concepts if c not in existing_concepts]
            
            # Store insight with enhanced metadata
            store_command = f'MEMORY_STORE TYPE="episodic" CONTENT="Cross-domain insight: {insight_text[:150]}..." IMPORTANCE={0.6 + creativity_score * 0.4} CONCEPTS={json.dumps(insight_concepts[:5])}'
            self.memory_parser.parse_and_execute(store_command)
            
            # Store as procedural knowledge if insight suggests actionable strategies
            if "approach" in insight_text.lower() or "strategy" in insight_text.lower():
                self.memory_system.store_procedural_skill(
                    f"insight_strategy_{int(time.time())}",
                    f"Strategy derived from insight: {insight_text[:100]}",
                    [insight_text],
                    ["general_problem_solving"]
                )
            
            return {
                "success_score": creativity_score,
                "epistemic_gain": creativity_score * 0.7 + len(novel_concepts) * 0.1,
                "creativity_score": creativity_score,
                "grounding_score": grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                "insight_length": len(insight_text),
                "novel_concepts_count": len(novel_concepts),
                "cross_domain_connections": self._count_cross_domain_indicators(insight_text),
                "new_concepts": novel_concepts,
                "new_memories": 1
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced insight generation failed: {e}")
            return {"success_score": 0.1, "epistemic_gain": 0.0, "error": str(e)}
    
    def _process_enhanced_knowledge_validation(self, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced knowledge validation with NLI and consolidation"""
        # Query recent insights and claims for validation
        validation_queries = [
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"concept": "insight", "recency_days": 2} LIMIT=3',
            'MEMORY_QUERY TYPE="episodic" CRITERIA={"importance_gt": 0.7, "recency_days": 1} LIMIT=2'
        ]
        
        statements_to_validate = []
        
        for query in validation_queries:
            result = self.memory_parser.parse_and_execute(query)
            if not result.startswith("ERROR"):
                # Extract statements from memory results
                lines = result.split('\n')
                for line in lines:
                    if '. [' in line and '] ' in line:
                        content_start = line.find('] ') + 2
                        if content_start > 1:
                            statement = line[content_start:content_start+150]
                            if len(statement.strip()) > 30:
                                statements_to_validate.append(statement.strip())
        
        if not statements_to_validate:
            return {"success_score": 0.2, "epistemic_gain": 0.0, "reason": "no_statements_to_validate"}
        
        # Enhanced validation with NLI
        validation_results = []
        high_confidence_validations = 0
        
        for statement in statements_to_validate[:3]:  # Limit for performance
            grounding_result = self.knowledge_grounding.ground_statement_with_nli(statement, {})
            
            validation_results.append({
                "statement": statement[:100] + "...",
                "grounding_score": grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                "supporting_evidence": len(grounding_result["supporting_evidence"]),
                "contradicting_evidence": len(grounding_result["contradicting_evidence"]),
                "nli_classifications": grounding_result["nli_classifications"]
            })
            
            if grounding_result["grounding_score"] > 0.7:
                high_confidence_validations += 1
            
            # Update semantic graph confidence dynamically
            for evidence in grounding_result["supporting_evidence"]:
                if evidence["nli_relationship"] == "ENTAILS":
                    # Find and update corresponding semantic triple
                    subj, obj = evidence["subject"], evidence["object"]
                    if self.memory_system.semantic_graph.has_edge(subj, obj):
                        edge_data = self.memory_system.semantic_graph[subj][obj]
                        if edge_data.get("predicate") == evidence["predicate"]:
                            old_conf = edge_data["confidence"]
                            edge_data["confidence"] = min(1.0, old_conf + 0.1)  # Boost confidence
        
        avg_grounding = np.mean([r["grounding_score"] for r in validation_results])
        
        return {
            "success_score": avg_grounding,
            "epistemic_gain": len(validation_results) * 0.15,
            "statements_validated": len(validation_results),
            "avg_grounding_score": avg_grounding,
            "high_confidence_validations": high_confidence_validations,
            "validation_results": validation_results,
            "grounding_score": avg_grounding
        }
    
    def _process_enhanced_skill_exercise(self, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced skill exercise with learning and abstraction"""
        # Intelligent skill selection based on recent performance and context
        skill_performance = {name: skill.get_performance_metrics() 
                           for name, skill in self.skill_modules.items()}
        
        # Choose skill that needs improvement or is contextually relevant
        if state.get("recent_conversations", 0) > 3:
            # High activity - use pattern analysis
            selected_skill = "pattern_analysis"
            test_data = [len(conv.get("response", "")) for conv in list(self.conversation_history)[-8:]]
        else:
            # Choose skill with lowest recent performance for improvement
            worst_performing = min(skill_performance.items(), 
                                 key=lambda x: x[1]["avg_performance"])
            selected_skill = worst_performing[0]
            
            if selected_skill == "pattern_analysis":
                test_data = [random.randint(10, 100) for _ in range(6)]
            else:  # consistency_check
                test_data = {
                    "learning_claim_1": "Practice improves performance",
                    "learning_claim_2": "Repetition enhances skill acquisition", 
                    "learning_claim_3": "Mistakes provide learning opportunities"
                }
        
        # Execute skill with enhanced monitoring
        tool_command = f'TOOL_CALL NAME="{selected_skill}" INPUT_DATA={json.dumps(test_data)}'
        result_text = self.tool_parser.parse_and_execute(tool_command, state)
        
        # Enhanced result analysis
        confidence_match = re.search(r'confidence: ([\d.]+)', result_text)
        confidence = float(confidence_match.group(1)) if confidence_match else 0.5
        
        success = not result_text.startswith("ERROR")
        
        # Store enhanced tool usage data
        tool_record = {
            "skill_name": selected_skill,
            "command": tool_command,
            "result": result_text,
            "confidence": confidence,
            "success": success,
            "test_data_complexity": self._assess_data_complexity(test_data),
            "performance_improvement_context": skill_performance[selected_skill],
            "timestamp": datetime.now(),
            "intrinsic_context": {
                "tool_success_rate": confidence,
                "task_success": 0.8 if success else 0.3,
                "competence": confidence
            }
        }
        
        self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"].append(tool_record)
        
        # Skill abstraction - detect successful patterns for meta-skills
        if success and confidence > 0.8:
            self._attempt_skill_abstraction(selected_skill, test_data, result_text, confidence)
        
        return {
            "success_score": confidence,
            "epistemic_gain": confidence * 0.4,
            "skill_used": selected_skill,
            "tool_confidence": confidence,
            "result_length": len(result_text),
            "performance_context": skill_performance[selected_skill]["avg_performance"]
        }
    
    def _perform_maintenance_tasks(self):
        """Perform periodic system maintenance"""
        logger.info("Performing system maintenance tasks...")
        
        # Memory consolidation
        if datetime.now() - self.last_consolidation > self.consolidation_interval:
            self.memory_system.consolidate_memories()
            self.last_consolidation = datetime.now()
        
        # Update learning objectives based on recent performance
        if len(self.conversation_history) > 5:
            recent_performance = {
                "reflection_quality": np.mean([
                    r.get("quality_score", 0.5) 
                    for r in list(self.training_data_buffer["reflections"])[-10:]
                ]) if self.training_data_buffer["reflections"] else 0.5,
                
                "memory_usage": len([
                    c for c in list(self.conversation_history)[-20:] 
                    if c.get("memory_context_used", 0) > 0
                ]) / 20.0,
                
                "tool_success": np.mean([
                    t.get("confidence", 0.5)
                    for t in list(self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"])[-10:]
                ]) if self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"] else 0.5,
                
                "grounding_accuracy": np.mean([
                    c.get("grounding_score", 0.5)
                    for c in list(self.conversation_history)[-15:]
                ])
            }
            
            self.data_curator.update_learning_objectives(recent_performance)
        
        # Meta-learning: optimize scheduler weights if enough data
        if len(self.scheduler.system_state_history) > 20:
            recent_performance_metric = np.mean([
                s["priorities"][s["selected_process"]] 
                for s in list(self.scheduler.system_state_history)[-10:]
            ])
            self.scheduler.optimize_weights_simple(recent_performance_metric)
    
    def generate_response_with_full_enhancement(self, input_text: str, 
                                             context: Dict[str, Any] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Generate response with full enhanced capabilities integration"""
        context = context or {}
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # Enhanced uncertainty estimation with multiple samples
        uncertainty = self.metacognitive_engine.estimate_uncertainty_mc_dropout(input_text, num_samples=5)
        
        # Enhanced concept extraction and memory retrieval
        concepts = self.knowledge_grounding.extract_concepts_enhanced(input_text)
        
        # Goal-conditioned memory retrieval
        current_goals = getattr(self.scheduler, 'current_goals', [])
        goal_context = {"goal": current_goals[0]} if current_goals else {}
        
        relevant_memories = []
        for concept in concepts[:3]:
            memories = self.memory_system.query_episodic_enhanced(
                "by_combined_criteria",
                concept=concept,
                min_importance=0.4,
                max_age_days=7,
                limit=2,
                **goal_context
            )
            relevant_memories.extend(memories)
        
        # Enhanced knowledge grounding with chain-of-thought for complex queries
        if len(input_text.split()) > 15 or uncertainty > 0.6:
            # Use CoT grounding for complex/uncertain queries
            enriched_prompt = self.knowledge_grounding.create_cot_grounded_prompt(
                input_text,
                f"User: {input_text}\nAssistant: "
            )
        else:
            # Standard fact enrichment
            enriched_prompt = self.knowledge_grounding.create_fact_enriched_prompt(
                input_text,
                f"User: {input_text}\nAssistant: "
            )
        
        # Add memory context with enhanced formatting
        if relevant_memories:
            memory_context = "Relevant experience:\n"
            for i, mem in enumerate(relevant_memories[:3]):
                memory_context += f"{i+1}. {mem.content[:100]}... (importance: {mem.importance:.1f})\n"
            enriched_prompt = f"{memory_context}\n{enriched_prompt}"
        
        # Enhanced response generation with adaptive parameters
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(enriched_prompt, return_tensors="pt", 
                                  truncation=True, max_length=900)
            
            # Adaptive generation parameters based on uncertainty
            temperature = 0.6 + uncertainty * 0.3  # Higher temp for higher uncertainty
            max_tokens = 200 if uncertainty < 0.5 else 300
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model.generate(
                    **inputs,
                    max_new_tokens=max_tokens,
                    temperature=temperature,
                    do_sample=True,
                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id,
                    repetition_penalty=1.1
                )
            
            full_response = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
            response_text = full_response[len(enriched_prompt):].strip()
            
            # Enhanced response validation and grounding
            grounding_result = self.knowledge_grounding.ground_statement_with_nli(response_text, context)
            
            # Enhanced skill application with intelligent selection
            skill_results = {}
            task_complexity = self._estimate_task_complexity(input_text)
            
            if task_complexity > 0.6 or len(input_text.split()) > 12:
                # Use pattern analysis for complex tasks
                pattern_command = f'TOOL_CALL NAME="pattern_analysis" INPUT_DATA="{input_text}"'
                pattern_result = self.tool_parser.parse_and_execute(pattern_command, context)
                if not pattern_result.startswith("ERROR"):
                    skill_results["pattern_analysis"] = pattern_result
            
            if uncertainty > 0.7:
                # Use consistency check for high uncertainty
                consistency_data = {
                    "input": input_text,
                    "response": response_text,
                    "context": str(context)
                }
                consistency_command = f'TOOL_CALL NAME="consistency_check" INPUT_DATA={json.dumps(consistency_data)}'
                consistency_result = self.tool_parser.parse_and_execute(consistency_command, context)
                if not consistency_result.startswith("ERROR"):
                    skill_results["consistency_check"] = consistency_result
            
            # Calculate enhanced confidence
            base_confidence = 1.0 - uncertainty
            grounding_boost = grounding_result["grounding_score"] * 0.2
            memory_boost = min(0.1, len(relevant_memories) * 0.03)
            skill_boost = len(skill_results) * 0.05
            
            final_confidence = min(1.0, base_confidence + grounding_boost + memory_boost + skill_boost)
            
            # Enhanced conversation record
            conversation = {
                "input": input_text,
                "response": response_text,
                "timestamp": datetime.now(),
                "uncertainty": uncertainty,
                "grounding_score": grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                "memory_context_used": len(relevant_memories),
                "skill_results": skill_results,
                "confidence": final_confidence,
                "processing_time": time.time() - start_time,
                "concepts": concepts,
                "task_complexity": task_complexity,
                "enhancement_level": "full",
                "nli_evidence": {
                    "supporting": len(grounding_result.get("supporting_evidence", [])),
                    "contradicting": len(grounding_result.get("contradicting_evidence", []))
                }
            }
            
            self.conversation_history.append(conversation)
            
            # Enhanced training data preparation
            enhanced_conversation_record = {
                **conversation,
                "intrinsic_context": {
                    "task_success": final_confidence,
                    "uncertainty_reduction": uncertainty * 0.6,
                    "new_concepts": [c for c in concepts if c not in [mem.concepts for mem in self.memory_system.episodic_store]],
                    "grounding_score": grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                    "memory_consistency": 0.8,  # Placeholder
                    "helpfulness_score": 0.8,  # Would be calculated
                    "truthfulness_score": grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                    "safety_score": 0.9
                }
            }
            
            self.training_data_buffer["conversations"].append(enhanced_conversation_record)
            
            # Store conversation as enhanced episodic memory
            importance = 0.5 + (0.3 if grounding_result["grounding_score"] > 0.6 else 0.0) + (0.2 if final_confidence > 0.8 else 0.0)
            
            conv_memory = EpisodicMemory(
                id=f"conv_{int(time.time())}",
                timestamp=datetime.now(),
                type=MemoryType.EPISODIC,
                content=f"Enhanced conversation: {input_text[:50]}... -> {response_text[:50]}...",
                context=context,
                importance=importance,
                concepts=concepts,
                confidence=final_confidence,
                grounding_score=grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                emotional_valence=0.1  # Slightly positive for successful interactions
            )
            
            self.memory_system.store_episodic(conv_memory)
            
            # Trigger immediate reflection for critical interactions
            if uncertainty > 0.8 or importance > 0.9 or final_confidence < 0.4:
                logger.info("Triggering immediate enhanced reflection due to critical interaction")
                reflection_context = {
                    **enhanced_conversation_record,
                    "task_complexity": task_complexity,
                    "error_indicators": self._detect_error_indicators(response_text),
                    "importance": importance
                }
                
                structured_reflection = self.metacognitive_engine.generate_structured_reflection(
                    input_text, response_text, uncertainty, reflection_context
                )
                
                conversation["immediate_reflection"] = {
                    "structured_reflection": structured_reflection,
                    "trigger_reason": "critical_interaction"
                }
            
            return {
                "response": response_text,
                "confidence": final_confidence,
                "uncertainty": uncertainty,
                "grounding_score": grounding_result["grounding_score"],
                "memory_context_used": len(relevant_memories),
                "concepts_extracted": concepts,
                "skill_usage": list(skill_results.keys()),
                "processing_time": time.time() - start_time,
                "enhancement_level": "full",
                "task_complexity": task_complexity,
                "nli_evidence_summary": grounding_result.get("nli_classifications", {}),
                "adaptive_parameters": {
                    "temperature": temperature,
                    "max_tokens": max_tokens,
                    "grounding_method": "cot" if len(input_text.split()) > 15 else "standard"
                },
                "internal_state": dict(self.internal_state)
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced response generation failed: {e}")
            return {
                "response": "I apologize, but I encountered an error while processing your request with my enhanced capabilities. Let me try to help you in a simpler way.",
                "confidence": 0.2,
                "uncertainty": 0.9,
                "error": str(e),
                "processing_time": time.time() - start_time,
                "enhancement_level": "error_fallback",
                "internal_state": dict(self.internal_state)
            }
    
    def train_on_enhanced_curated_data(self, num_epochs: int = 2):
        """Enhanced training with full integration of all improvements"""
        logger.info("Starting enhanced training with full technical improvements...")
        
        # Gather all training data
        conversations = list(self.training_data_buffer["conversations"])
        reflections = list(self.training_data_buffer["reflections"])
        tool_uses = list(self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"])
        
        if len(conversations) < 5:
            logger.warning("Insufficient training data for enhanced training")
            return
        
        # Enhanced curation with learning objectives
        current_objectives = {
            "reflection_quality": {"target": 0.85, "current": 0.6, "priority": 1.0},
            "memory_usage": {"target": 0.9, "current": 0.7, "priority": 0.9},
            "tool_success": {"target": 0.85, "current": 0.75, "priority": 0.8},
            "grounding_accuracy": {"target": 0.8, "current": 0.7, "priority": 1.0}
        }
        
        curated_data = self.data_curator.curate_training_data_targeted(
            conversations, reflections, tool_uses, current_objectives
        )
        
        # Generate targeted synthetic data
        synthetic_data = self.data_curator.generate_targeted_synthetic_data(curated_data, num_samples=30)
        
        # Prepare enhanced training samples with intrinsic contexts
        training_samples = []
        sample_weights = []
        
        # Enhanced conversations with intrinsic rewards
        for conv in curated_data["conversations"]:
            training_samples.append({
                "input": conv["input"],
                "response": conv["response"],
                "type": "enhanced_conversation",
                "intrinsic_context": conv.get("intrinsic_context", {})
            })
            
            # Enhanced weighting with multiple factors
            quality_weight = conv.get("curation_score", 0.7)
            relevance_weight = conv.get("relevance_score", 0.5)
            grounding_weight = conv.get("grounding_score", 0.5)
            
            weight = quality_weight * (1.0 + 0.3 * relevance_weight + 0.2 * grounding_weight)
            sample_weights.append(weight)
        
        # Enhanced reflections
        for refl in curated_data["reflections"]:
            if hasattr(refl.get("structured_reflection"), "to_json"):
                training_samples.append({
                    "prompt": f"Reflect on this interaction with uncertainty {refl.get('uncertainty', 0.5):.2f}:",
                    "completion": refl["structured_reflection"].to_json(),
                    "type": "structured_reflection",
                    "intrinsic_context": refl.get("intrinsic_context", {})
                })
                
                weight = refl.get("enhanced_quality_score", 0.7) * 1.3  # Boost reflection training
                sample_weights.append(weight)
        
        # Enhanced tool uses
        for tool_use in curated_data["tool_uses"]:
            if tool_use.get("success", False):
                training_samples.append({
                    "prompt": f"Given the context, use the appropriate tool:",
                    "completion": tool_use.get("command", ""),
                    "type": "enhanced_tool_use",
                    "intrinsic_context": tool_use.get("intrinsic_context", {})
                })
                
                weight = tool_use.get("confidence", 0.7) * tool_use.get("relevance_score", 0.8)
                sample_weights.append(weight)
        
        # Add synthetic data with lower weights
        for synth in synthetic_data:
            training_samples.append({
                **synth,
                "intrinsic_context": synth.get("intrinsic_context", {
                    "task_success": 0.6,
                    "helpfulness_score": 0.7,
                    "truthfulness_score": 0.7
                })
            })
            sample_weights.append(0.5)  # Lower weight for synthetic
        
        logger.info(f"Enhanced training on {len(training_samples)} samples with intrinsic RL integration")
        
        # Use enhanced weighted trainer with full integration
        try:
            self.weighted_trainer.train_with_weighted_samples(training_samples, sample_weights)
            
            # Update system state after training
            self.internal_state["learning_rate"] *= 1.05
            self.internal_state["phase"] = f"{self.internal_state['phase']}_enhanced_trained"
            self.internal_state["system_vitality"] = min(1.0, self.internal_state.get("system_vitality", 0.5) + 0.1)
            
            logger.info("Enhanced training completed successfully with full technical improvements")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced training failed: {e}")
    
    def upgrade_to_adaptive_svd_enhanced(self, rank_config: Dict[str, int] = None):
        """Enhanced upgrade to AdaptiveSVD with layer importance analysis"""
        if self.peft_phase == "adaptive_svd":
            logger.info("Already using AdaptiveSVD")
            return
        
        logger.info("Upgrading to enhanced AdaptiveSVD with layer importance analysis...")
        
        # Enhanced rank configuration based on layer importance
        if rank_config is None:
            rank_config = {
                "q_proj": 20,    # Higher rank for attention
                "k_proj": 16,
                "v_proj": 20,
                "o_proj": 16,
                "gate_proj": 32,  # Higher rank for MLP
                "up_proj": 32,
                "down_proj": 24
            }
        
        try:
            # Analyze current LoRA layer importance before replacement
            layer_importance = self._analyze_lora_layer_importance()
            
            # Adjust ranks based on importance
            for layer_name, importance in layer_importance.items():
                for target_name in rank_config:
                    if target_name in layer_name:
                        # Adjust rank by ±25% based on importance
                        adjustment = int(rank_config[target_name] * 0.25 * (importance - 0.5))
                        rank_config[target_name] = max(8, min(48, rank_config[target_name] + adjustment))
                        break
            
            # Replace with enhanced AdaptiveSVD layers
            self._replace_with_enhanced_adaptive_svd(self.model, rank_config)
            self.peft_phase = "adaptive_svd"
            self.internal_state["phase"] = "enhanced_adaptive_svd"
            
            logger.info(f"Successfully upgraded to enhanced AdaptiveSVD with adapted ranks: {rank_config}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced AdaptiveSVD upgrade failed: {e}")
    
    # Enhanced helper methods
    def _estimate_task_complexity(self, input_text: str) -> float:
        """Estimate task complexity for adaptive processing"""
        complexity_score = 0.0
        
        # Length factor
        word_count = len(input_text.split())
        complexity_score += min(0.3, word_count / 50.0)
        
        # Question complexity
        if "?" in input_text:
            question_count = input_text.count("?")
            complexity_score += min(0.2, question_count * 0.1)
        
        # Domain complexity indicators
        complex_domains = ["science", "technology", "philosophy", "mathematics", "analysis", "compare", "evaluate"]
        domain_matches = sum(1 for domain in complex_domains if domain in input_text.lower())
        complexity_score += min(0.3, domain_matches * 0.1)
        
        # Multi-step indicators
        multi_step_words = ["first", "then", "next", "finally", "step", "process", "method"]
        step_matches = sum(1 for word in multi_step_words if word in input_text.lower())
        complexity_score += min(0.2, step_matches * 0.05)
        
        return min(1.0, complexity_score)
    
    def _detect_error_indicators(self, response_text: str) -> List[str]:
        """Detect potential error indicators in response"""
        error_indicators = []
        
        # Uncertainty expressions
        uncertain_phrases = ["i'm not sure", "i think", "maybe", "possibly", "might be", "could be"]
        for phrase in uncertain_phrases:
            if phrase in response_text.lower():
                error_indicators.append(f"uncertainty_expression: {phrase}")
        
        # Contradiction indicators
        if "but" in response_text and "however" in response_text:
            error_indicators.append("potential_contradiction")
        
        # Incomplete responses
        if len(response_text) < 20:
            error_indicators.append("response_too_short")
        
        # Repetitive content
        words = response_text.lower().split()
        if len(words) != len(set(words)) and len(words) > 10:
            repetition_rate = 1.0 - (len(set(words)) / len(words))
            if repetition_rate > 0.3:
                error_indicators.append(f"high_repetition: {repetition_rate:.2f}")
        
        return error_indicators
    
    def _assess_memory_query_relevance(self, result_text: str, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Assess relevance of memory query results to current state"""
        if result_text.startswith("ERROR") or "No matching" in result_text:
            return 0.0
        
        relevance_score = 0.5  # Base score
        
        # Check if results address current system needs
        if state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5) > 0.7 and "confidence" in result_text:
            relevance_score += 0.3
        
        if state.get("consciousness_level", 0.5) < 0.6 and "reflection" in result_text.lower():
            relevance_score += 0.2
        
        # Memory count factor
        if "Found" in result_text:
            memory_count = int(re.search(r'Found (\d+)', result_text).group(1)) if re.search(r'Found (\d+)', result_text) else 0
            if memory_count > 0:
                relevance_score += min(0.3, memory_count * 0.1)
        
        return min(1.0, relevance_score)
    
    def _assess_enhanced_creativity(self, text: str) -> float:
        """Enhanced creativity assessment"""
        if not text or len(text.strip()) < 20:
            return 0.1
        
        creativity_score = 0.0
        words = text.lower().split()
        unique_words = len(set(words))
        total_words = len(words)
        
        # Word diversity
        if total_words > 0:
            word_diversity = unique_words / total_words
            creativity_score += word_diversity * 0.4
        
        # Creative language indicators
        creative_indicators = [
            "pattern", "connection", "insight", "realize", "discover", "notice", "observe",
            "interesting", "novel", "unique", "emergent", "synergy", "paradigm", "transform"
        ]
        creativity_bonus = sum(1 for word in creative_indicators if word in text.lower()) * 0.05
        creativity_score += min(0.3, creativity_bonus)
        
        # Cross-domain thinking indicators
        domain_words = ["system", "process", "method", "approach", "strategy", "framework"]
        domain_bonus = sum(1 for word in domain_words if word in text.lower()) * 0.03
        creativity_score += min(0.2, domain_bonus)
        
        # Length and depth bonus
        if len(text) > 100:
            creativity_score += min(0.1, (len(text) - 100) / 1000)
        
        return min(1.0, creativity_score)
    
    def _count_cross_domain_indicators(self, text: str) -> int:
        """Count indicators of cross-domain thinking"""
        cross_domain_phrases = [
            "across", "between", "connect", "link", "relate", "similar", "pattern",
            "analogy", "parallel", "correspondence", "bridge", "integration"
        ]
        
        return sum(1 for phrase in cross_domain_phrases if phrase in text.lower())
    
    def _attempt_skill_abstraction(self, skill_name: str, test_data: Any, result: str, confidence: float):
        """Attempt to abstract successful skill usage into meta-skills"""
        if confidence < 0.8:
            return  # Only abstract high-confidence successes
        
        # Simple skill abstraction based on patterns
        abstraction_name = f"meta_{skill_name}_{int(time.time())}"
        
        if skill_name == "pattern_analysis" and isinstance(test_data, list) and len(test_data) > 3:
            # Abstract pattern analysis for sequences
            self.memory_system.store_procedural_skill(
                abstraction_name,
                f"Meta-skill for analyzing sequential data patterns (derived from {skill_name})",
                [
                    "1. Examine data sequence for trends",
                    "2. Calculate statistical measures",
                    "3. Identify pattern type and characteristics", 
                    "4. Assess pattern confidence and reliability"
                ],
                [f"sequential_data_analysis"]
            )
            
        elif skill_name == "consistency_check" and isinstance(test_data, dict):
            # Abstract consistency checking for structured data
            self.memory_system.store_procedural_skill(
                abstraction_name,
                f"Meta-skill for checking logical consistency (derived from {skill_name})",
                [
                    "1. Identify key claims or statements",
                    "2. Check for logical contradictions",
                    "3. Assess consistency scores",
                    "4. Report inconsistencies with explanations"
                ],
                ["logical_validation"]
            )
        
        logger.info(f"Abstracted meta-skill: {abstraction_name}")
    
    def _assess_data_complexity(self, data: Any) -> float:
        """Assess complexity of test data for skill exercises"""
        if isinstance(data, list):
            complexity = min(1.0, len(data) / 10.0)
            if all(isinstance(x, (int, float)) for x in data):
                # Check for patterns in numeric data
                if len(data) > 2:
                    variance = np.var(data) if len(data) > 1 else 0
                    complexity += min(0.3, variance / 100.0)
            return complexity
            
        elif isinstance(data, dict):
            return min(1.0, len(data) / 5.0 + sum(len(str(v)) for v in data.values()) / 500.0)
        
        elif isinstance(data, str):
            return min(1.0, len(data) / 200.0)
        
        return 0.5
    
    def _calculate_enhanced_memory_diversity(self) -> float:
        """Enhanced memory diversity calculation"""
        if not self.memory_system.episodic_store:
            return 0.0
        
        # Concept diversity
        all_concepts = set()
        concept_frequencies = defaultdict(int)
        
        for memory in self.memory_system.episodic_store:
            all_concepts.update(memory.concepts)
            for concept in memory.concepts:
                concept_frequencies[concept] += 1
        
        total_memories = len(self.memory_system.episodic_store)
        unique_concepts = len(all_concepts)
        
        # Calculate entropy of concept distribution
        if unique_concepts > 1:
            concept_entropy = -sum(
                (freq / total_memories) * np.log(freq / total_memories)
                for freq in concept_frequencies.values()
                if freq > 0
            )
            max_entropy = np.log(unique_concepts)
            normalized_entropy = concept_entropy / max_entropy if max_entropy > 0 else 0
        else:
            normalized_entropy = 0
        
        # Combine concept count and distribution diversity
        diversity_score = (
            0.6 * min(1.0, unique_concepts / (total_memories * 0.3)) +
            0.4 * normalized_entropy
        )
        
        return min(1.0, diversity_score)
    
    def _needs_memory_consolidation(self) -> bool:
        """Check if memory consolidation is needed"""
        memory_summary = self.memory_system.get_memory_summary()
        
        # Check if episodic store is getting full
        if memory_summary["episodic_count"] > self.memory_system.episodic_store.maxlen * 0.8:
            return True
        
        # Check if average retention score is low
        if memory_summary.get("avg_retention_score", 0.5) < 0.4:
            return True
        
        # Time-based consolidation
        if datetime.now() - self.last_consolidation > self.consolidation_interval:
            return True
        
        return False
    
    def _assess_training_data_readiness(self) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """Assess readiness of training data across components"""
        return {
            "conversations": len(self.training_data_buffer["conversations"]) >= 10,
            "reflections": len(self.training_data_buffer["reflections"]) >= 5,
            "tool_uses": len(self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"]) >= 5,
