                "processing_time": time.time() - start_time,
                "enhancement_level": "error_fallback",
                "internal_state": dict(self.internal_state)
            }
    
    def train_on_enhanced_curated_data(self, num_epochs: int = 2):
        """Enhanced training with full integration of all improvements"""
        logger.info("Starting enhanced training with full technical improvements...")
        
        # Gather all training data
        conversations = list(self.training_data_buffer["conversations"])
        reflections = list(self.training_data_buffer["reflections"])
        tool_uses = list(self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"])
        
        if len(conversations) < 5:
            logger.warning("Insufficient training data for enhanced training")
            return
        
        # Enhanced curation with learning objectives
        current_objectives = {
            "reflection_quality": {"target": 0.85, "current": 0.6, "priority": 1.0},
            "memory_usage": {"target": 0.9, "current": 0.7, "priority": 0.9},
            "tool_success": {"target": 0.85, "current": 0.75, "priority": 0.8},
            "grounding_accuracy": {"target": 0.8, "current": 0.7, "priority": 1.0}
        }
        
        curated_data = self.data_curator.curate_training_data_targeted(
            conversations, reflections, tool_uses, current_objectives
        )
        
        # Generate targeted synthetic data
        synthetic_data = self.data_curator.generate_targeted_synthetic_data(curated_data, num_samples=30)
        
        # Prepare enhanced training samples with intrinsic contexts
        training_samples = []
        sample_weights = []
        
        # Enhanced conversations with intrinsic rewards
        for conv in curated_data["conversations"]:
            training_samples.append({
                "input": conv["input"],
                "response": conv["response"],
                "type": "enhanced_conversation",
                "intrinsic_context": conv.get("intrinsic_context", {})
            })
            
            # Enhanced weighting with multiple factors
            quality_weight = conv.get("curation_score", 0.7)
            relevance_weight = conv.get("relevance_score", 0.5)
            grounding_weight = conv.get("grounding_score", 0.5)
            
            weight = quality_weight * (1.0 + 0.3 * relevance_weight + 0.2 * grounding_weight)
            sample_weights.append(weight)
        
        # Enhanced reflections
        for refl in curated_data["reflections"]:
            if hasattr(refl.get("structured_reflection"), "to_json"):
                training_samples.append({
                    "prompt": f"Reflect on this interaction with uncertainty {refl.get('uncertainty', 0.5):.2f}:",
                    "completion": refl["structured_reflection"].to_json(),
                    "type": "structured_reflection",
                    "intrinsic_context": refl.get("intrinsic_context", {})
                })
                
                weight = refl.get("enhanced_quality_score", 0.7) * 1.3  # Boost reflection training
                sample_weights.append(weight)
        
        # Enhanced tool uses
        for tool_use in curated_data["tool_uses"]:
            if tool_use.get("success", False):
                training_samples.append({
                    "prompt": f"Given the context, use the appropriate tool:",
                    "completion": tool_use.get("command", ""),
                    "type": "enhanced_tool_use",
                    "intrinsic_context": tool_use.get("intrinsic_context", {})
                })
                
                weight = tool_use.get("confidence", 0.7) * tool_use.get("relevance_score", 0.8)
                sample_weights.append(weight)
        
        # Add synthetic data with lower weights
        for synth in synthetic_data:
            training_samples.append({
                **synth,
                "intrinsic_context": synth.get("intrinsic_context", {
                    "task_success": 0.6,
                    "helpfulness_score": 0.7,
                    "truthfulness_score": 0.7
                })
            })
            sample_weights.append(0.5)  # Lower weight for synthetic
        
        logger.info(f"Enhanced training on {len(training_samples)} samples with intrinsic RL integration")
        
        # Use enhanced weighted trainer with full integration
        try:
            self.weighted_trainer.train_with_weighted_samples(training_samples, sample_weights)
            
            # Update system state after training
            self.internal_state["learning_rate"] *= 1.05
            self.internal_state["phase"] = f"{self.internal_state['phase']}_enhanced_trained"
            self.internal_state["system_vitality"] = min(1.0, self.internal_state.get("system_vitality", 0.5) + 0.1)
            
            logger.info("Enhanced training completed successfully with full technical improvements")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced training failed: {e}")
    
    def upgrade_to_adaptive_svd_enhanced(self, rank_config: Dict[str, int] = None):
        """Enhanced upgrade to AdaptiveSVD with layer importance analysis"""
        if self.peft_phase == "adaptive_svd":
            logger.info("Already using AdaptiveSVD")
            return
        
        logger.info("Upgrading to enhanced AdaptiveSVD with layer importance analysis...")
        
        # Enhanced rank configuration based on layer importance
        if rank_config is None:
            rank_config = {
                "q_proj": 20,    # Higher rank for attention
                "k_proj": 16,
                "v_proj": 20,
                "o_proj": 16,
                "gate_proj": 32,  # Higher rank for MLP
                "up_proj": 32,
                "down_proj": 24
            }
        
        try:
            # Analyze current LoRA layer importance before replacement
            layer_importance = self._analyze_lora_layer_importance()
            
            # Adjust ranks based on importance
            for layer_name, importance in layer_importance.items():
                for target_name in rank_config:
                    if target_name in layer_name:
                        # Adjust rank by ±25% based on importance
                        adjustment = int(rank_config[target_name] * 0.25 * (importance - 0.5))
                        rank_config[target_name] = max(8, min(48, rank_config[target_name] + adjustment))
                        break
            
            # Replace with enhanced AdaptiveSVD layers
            self._replace_with_enhanced_adaptive_svd(self.model, rank_config)
            self.peft_phase = "adaptive_svd"
            self.internal_state["phase"] = "enhanced_adaptive_svd"
            
            logger.info(f"Successfully upgraded to enhanced AdaptiveSVD with adapted ranks: {rank_config}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced AdaptiveSVD upgrade failed: {e}")
    
    # Enhanced helper methods
    def _estimate_task_complexity(self, input_text: str) -> float:
        """Estimate task complexity for adaptive processing"""
        complexity_score = 0.0
        
        # Length factor
        word_count = len(input_text.split())
        complexity_score += min(0.3, word_count / 50.0)
        
        # Question complexity
        if "?" in input_text:
            question_count = input_text.count("?")
            complexity_score += min(0.2, question_count * 0.1)
        
        # Domain complexity indicators
        complex_domains = ["science", "technology", "philosophy", "mathematics", "analysis", "compare", "evaluate"]
        domain_matches = sum(1 for domain in complex_domains if domain in input_text.lower())
        complexity_score += min(0.3, domain_matches * 0.1)
        
        # Multi-step indicators
        multi_step_words = ["first", "then", "next", "finally", "step", "process", "method"]
        step_matches = sum(1 for word in multi_step_words if word in input_text.lower())
        complexity_score += min(0.2, step_matches * 0.05)
        
        return min(1.0, complexity_score)
    
    def _detect_error_indicators(self, response_text: str) -> List[str]:
        """Detect potential error indicators in response"""
        error_indicators = []
        
        # Uncertainty expressions
        uncertain_phrases = ["i'm not sure", "i think", "maybe", "possibly", "might be", "could be"]
        for phrase in uncertain_phrases:
            if phrase in response_text.lower():
                error_indicators.append(f"uncertainty_expression: {phrase}")
        
        # Contradiction indicators
        if "but" in response_text and "however" in response_text:
            error_indicators.append("potential_contradiction")
        
        # Incomplete responses
        if len(response_text) < 20:
            error_indicators.append("response_too_short")
        
        # Repetitive content
        words = response_text.lower().split()
        if len(words) != len(set(words)) and len(words) > 10:
            repetition_rate = 1.0 - (len(set(words)) / len(words))
            if repetition_rate > 0.3:
                error_indicators.append(f"high_repetition: {repetition_rate:.2f}")
        
        return error_indicators
    
    def _assess_memory_query_relevance(self, result_text: str, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Assess relevance of memory query results to current state"""
        if result_text.startswith("ERROR") or "No matching" in result_text:
            return 0.0
        
        relevance_score = 0.5  # Base score
        
        # Check if results address current system needs
        if state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5) > 0.7 and "confidence" in result_text:
            relevance_score += 0.3
        
        if state.get("consciousness_level", 0.5) < 0.6 and "reflection" in result_text.lower():
            relevance_score += 0.2
        
        # Memory count factor
        if "Found" in result_text:
            memory_count = int(re.search(r'Found (\d+)', result_text).group(1)) if re.search(r'Found (\d+)', result_text) else 0
            if memory_count > 0:
                relevance_score += min(0.3, memory_count * 0.1)
        
        return min(1.0, relevance_score)
    
    def _assess_enhanced_creativity(self, text: str) -> float:
        """Enhanced creativity assessment"""
        if not text or len(text.strip()) < 20:
            return 0.1
        
        creativity_score = 0.0
        words = text.lower().split()
        unique_words = len(set(words))
        total_words = len(words)
        
        # Word diversity
        if total_words > 0:
            word_diversity = unique_words / total_words
            creativity_score += word_diversity * 0.4
        
        # Creative language indicators
        creative_indicators = [
            "pattern", "connection", "insight", "realize", "discover", "notice", "observe",
            "interesting", "novel", "unique", "emergent", "synergy", "paradigm", "transform"
        ]
        creativity_bonus = sum(1 for word in creative_indicators if word in text.lower()) * 0.05
        creativity_score += min(0.3, creativity_bonus)
        
        # Cross-domain thinking indicators
        domain_words = ["system", "process", "method", "approach", "strategy", "framework"]
        domain_bonus = sum(1 for word in domain_words if word in text.lower()) * 0.03
        creativity_score += min(0.2, domain_bonus)
        
        # Length and depth bonus
        if len(text) > 100:
            creativity_score += min(0.1, (len(text) - 100) / 1000)
        
        return min(1.0, creativity_score)
    
    def _count_cross_domain_indicators(self, text: str) -> int:
        """Count indicators of cross-domain thinking"""
        cross_domain_phrases = [
            "across", "between", "connect", "link", "relate", "similar", "pattern",
            "analogy", "parallel", "correspondence", "bridge", "integration"
        ]
        
        return sum(1 for phrase in cross_domain_phrases if phrase in text.lower())
    
    def _attempt_skill_abstraction(self, skill_name: str, test_data: Any, result: str, confidence: float):
        """Attempt to abstract successful skill usage into meta-skills"""
        if confidence < 0.8:
            return  # Only abstract high-confidence successes
        
        # Simple skill abstraction based on patterns
        abstraction_name = f"meta_{skill_name}_{int(time.time())}"
        
        if skill_name == "pattern_analysis" and isinstance(test_data, list) and len(test_data) > 3:
            # Abstract pattern analysis for sequences
            self.memory_system.store_procedural_skill(
                abstraction_name,
                f"Meta-skill for analyzing sequential data patterns (derived from {skill_name})",
                [
                    "1. Examine data sequence for trends",
                    "2. Calculate statistical measures",
                    "3. Identify pattern type and characteristics", 
                    "4. Assess pattern confidence and reliability"
                ],
                [f"sequential_data_analysis"]
            )
            
        elif skill_name == "consistency_check" and isinstance(test_data, dict):
            # Abstract consistency checking for structured data
            self.memory_system.store_procedural_skill(
                abstraction_name,
                f"Meta-skill for checking logical consistency (derived from {skill_name})",
                [
                    "1. Identify key claims or statements",
                    "2. Check for logical contradictions",
                    "3. Assess consistency scores",
                    "4. Report inconsistencies with explanations"
                ],
                ["logical_validation"]
            )
        
        logger.info(f"Abstracted meta-skill: {abstraction_name}")
    
    def _assess_data_complexity(self, data: Any) -> float:
        """Assess complexity of test data for skill exercises"""
        if isinstance(data, list):
            complexity = min(1.0, len(data) / 10.0)
            if all(isinstance(x, (int, float)) for x in data):
                # Check for patterns in numeric data
                if len(data) > 2:
                    variance = np.var(data) if len(data) > 1 else 0
                    complexity += min(0.3, variance / 100.0)
            return complexity
            
        elif isinstance(data, dict):
            return min(1.0, len(data) / 5.0 + sum(len(str(v)) for v in data.values()) / 500.0)
        
        elif isinstance(data, str):
            return min(1.0, len(data) / 200.0)
        
        return 0.5
    
    def _calculate_enhanced_memory_diversity(self) -> float:
        """Enhanced memory diversity calculation"""
        if not self.memory_system.episodic_store:
            return 0.0
        
        # Concept diversity
        all_concepts = set()
        concept_frequencies = defaultdict(int)
        
        for memory in self.memory_system.episodic_store:
            all_concepts.update(memory.concepts)
            for concept in memory.concepts:
                concept_frequencies[concept] += 1
        
        total_memories = len(self.memory_system.episodic_store)
        unique_concepts = len(all_concepts)
        
        # Calculate entropy of concept distribution
        if unique_concepts > 1:
            concept_entropy = -sum(
                (freq / total_memories) * np.log(freq / total_memories)
                for freq in concept_frequencies.values()
                if freq > 0
            )
            max_entropy = np.log(unique_concepts)
            normalized_entropy = concept_entropy / max_entropy if max_entropy > 0 else 0
        else:
            normalized_entropy = 0
        
        # Combine concept count and distribution diversity
        diversity_score = (
            0.6 * min(1.0, unique_concepts / (total_memories * 0.3)) +
            0.4 * normalized_entropy
        )
        
        return min(1.0, diversity_score)
    
    def _needs_memory_consolidation(self) -> bool:
        """Check if memory consolidation is needed"""
        memory_summary = self.memory_system.get_memory_summary()
        
        # Check if episodic store is getting full
        if memory_summary["episodic_count"] > self.memory_system.episodic_store.maxlen * 0.8:
            return True
        
        # Check if average retention score is low
        if memory_summary.get("avg_retention_score", 0.5) < 0.4:
            return True
        
        # Time-based consolidation
        if datetime.now() - self.last_consolidation > self.consolidation_interval:
            return True
        
        return False
    
    def _assess_training_data_readiness(self) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """Assess readiness of training data across components"""
        return {
            "conversations": len(self.training_data_buffer["conversations"]) >= 10,
            "reflections": len(self.training_data_buffer["reflections"]) >= 5,
            "tool_uses": len(self.training_data_buffer["tool_uses"]) >= 5,
            "overall": len(self.training_data_buffer["conversations"]) >= 15
        }
    
    def _analyze_lora_layer_importance(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Analyze LoRA layer importance for AdaptiveSVD rank adjustment"""
        layer_importance = {}
        
        # Simple importance analysis based on parameter magnitudes
        for name, module in self.model.named_modules():
            if hasattr(module, 'lora_A') and hasattr(module, 'lora_B'):
                # Calculate average parameter magnitude as proxy for importance
                lora_a_mag = torch.mean(torch.abs(module.lora_A.default.weight)).item()
                lora_b_mag = torch.mean(torch.abs(module.lora_B.default.weight)).item()
                
                # Combined importance score
                importance = (lora_a_mag + lora_b_mag) / 2.0
                layer_importance[name] = min(1.0, importance * 10)  # Scale to 0-1 range
        
        # Normalize importance scores
        if layer_importance:
            max_importance = max(layer_importance.values())
            if max_importance > 0:
                for name in layer_importance:
                    layer_importance[name] /= max_importance
        
        return layer_importance
    
    def _replace_with_enhanced_adaptive_svd(self, module, rank_config):
        """Replace layers with enhanced AdaptiveSVD"""
        for name, child_module in module.named_children():
            if isinstance(child_module, torch.nn.Linear):
                # Determine rank
                rank = 32  # Default
                for layer_type, layer_rank in rank_config.items():
                    if layer_type in name:
                        rank = layer_rank
                        break
                
                # Replace with enhanced AdaptiveSVD
                adaptive_layer = AdaptiveSVDLayer(child_module, rank=rank)
                setattr(module, name, adaptive_layer)
                logger.info(f"Replaced {name} with enhanced AdaptiveSVD (rank={rank})")
            else:
                self._replace_with_enhanced_adaptive_svd(child_module, rank_config)
    
    def _update_enhanced_internal_state(self, process_result: Dict[str, Any], system_vitality: float):
        """Enhanced internal state update with vitality feedback"""
        success_score = process_result.get("success_score", 0.5)
        
        # Vitality-modulated updates
        vitality_factor = 0.5 + 0.5 * system_vitality
        
        # Update consciousness level with vitality feedback
        consciousness_delta = 0.1 * success_score * vitality_factor
        self.internal_state["consciousness_level"] = min(1.0, 
            0.9 * self.internal_state["consciousness_level"] + consciousness_delta
        )
        
        # Update uncertainty level
        uncertainty_reduction = process_result.get("uncertainty_reduction", 0.0)
        if uncertainty_reduction > 0:
            self.internal_state["uncertainty_level"] = max(0.1, 
                self.internal_state["uncertainty_level"] - uncertainty_reduction * 0.1
            )
        
        # Adaptive learning rate based on system performance
        epistemic_gain = process_result.get("epistemic_gain", 0.0)
        if epistemic_gain > 0.2:
            self.internal_state["learning_rate"] = min(0.05, 
                self.internal_state["learning_rate"] * (1.0 + epistemic_gain)
            )
        
        # Update reflection frequency based on uncertainty
        self.internal_state["reflection_frequency"] = (
            0.05 + self.internal_state["uncertainty_level"] * 0.15
        )
    
    def get_comprehensive_enhanced_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get comprehensive enhanced system status"""
        return {
            "system_info": {
                "version": "Enhanced Digital Tom V4",
                "enhancement_level": self.enhancement_level,
                "peft_phase": self.peft_phase,
                "consciousness_active": self.consciousness_active,
                "model_parameters": sum(p.numel() for p in self.model.parameters()),
                "initialization_time": getattr(self, 'initialization_start', 0)
            },
            "internal_state": dict(self.internal_state),
            "system_vitality": self.internal_state.get("system_vitality", 0.5),
            "memory_system": self.memory_system.get_memory_summary(),
            "metacognitive_engine": self.metacognitive_engine.get_metacognitive_status(),
            "knowledge_grounding": self.knowledge_grounding.get_grounding_status(),
            "scheduler": self.scheduler.get_scheduling_status(),
            "data_curator": self.data_curator.get_curation_status(),
            "intrinsic_rewards": self.intrinsic_reward_calculator.get_reward_statistics(),
            "skill_modules": {name: skill.get_performance_metrics() 
                           for name, skill in self.skill_modules.items()},
            "training_data_readiness": self._assess_training_data_readiness(),
            "conversation_stats": {
                "total_conversations": len(self.conversation_history),
                "enhanced_conversations": len([c for c in self.conversation_history 
                                             if c.get("enhancement_level") == "full"]),
                "avg_confidence": np.mean([c.get("confidence", 0.5) for c in self.conversation_history]),
                "avg_grounding_score": np.mean([c.get("grounding_score", 0.5) for c in self.conversation_history]),
                "avg_task_complexity": np.mean([c.get("task_complexity", 0.5) for c in self.conversation_history if "task_complexity" in c])
            },
            "performance_metrics": {
                "avg_response_time": np.mean([c.get("processing_time", 1.0) for c in self.conversation_history]),
                "memory_usage_rate": len([c for c in self.conversation_history if c.get("memory_context_used", 0) > 0]) / max(1, len(self.conversation_history)),
                "skill_usage_rate": len([c for c in self.conversation_history if c.get("skill_results")]) / max(1, len(self.conversation_history)),
                "structured_reflection_rate": self.metacognitive_engine.get_metacognitive_status()["structured_success_rate"],
                "nli_evidence_avg": np.mean([
                    sum(c.get("nli_evidence_summary", {}).values()) 
                    for c in self.conversation_history 
                    if "nli_evidence_summary" in c
                ]) if any("nli_evidence_summary" in c for c in self.conversation_history) else 0.0
            },
            "learning_objectives": self.data_curator.learning_objectives,
            "maintenance_status": {
                "last_consolidation": self.last_consolidation,
                "consolidation_needed": self._needs_memory_consolidation(),
                "memory_diversity": self._calculate_enhanced_memory_diversity()
            }
        }

# Additional utility classes for completeness

class MemoryCommandParser:
    """
    Parser for structured text-based memory commands (from original implementation)
    Enhanced with better error handling and validation
    """
    
    def __init__(self, memory_system):
        self.memory_system = memory_system
        self.command_history = deque(maxlen=100)
        
    def parse_and_execute(self, command_text: str) -> str:
        """Parse memory command and execute it with enhanced validation"""
        try:
            command_text = command_text.strip()
            
            # Log command attempt
            self.command_history.append({
                "command": command_text,
                "timestamp": datetime.now()
            })
            
            if command_text.startswith("MEMORY_QUERY"):
                return self._handle_query(command_text)
            elif command_text.startswith("MEMORY_STORE"):
                return self._handle_store(command_text)
            else:
                return "ERROR: Unknown memory command format. Use MEMORY_QUERY or MEMORY_STORE"
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced memory command parsing error: {e}")
            return f"ERROR: Command execution failed - {str(e)}"
    
    def _handle_query(self, command: str) -> str:
        """Handle memory query commands with enhanced validation"""
        # Parse query parameters with better error handling
        type_match = re.search(r'TYPE="([^"]+)"', command)
        criteria_match = re.search(r'CRITERIA=(\{[^}]+\})', command)
        limit_match = re.search(r'LIMIT=(\d+)', command)
        
        if not type_match:
            return "ERROR: Query TYPE not specified. Use TYPE=\"episodic\" or TYPE=\"semantic\""
        
        query_type = type_match.group(1)
        limit = int(limit_match.group(1)) if limit_match else 5
        
        # Validate limit
        if limit > 20:
            limit = 20
            logger.warning("Query limit capped at 20 for performance")
        
        # Enhanced criteria parsing
        criteria = {}
        if criteria_match:
            try:
                criteria_str = criteria_match.group(1).replace("'", '"')
                criteria = json.loads(criteria_str)
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                return f"ERROR: Invalid criteria JSON format - {str(e)}"
        
        # Execute enhanced query
        try:
            if query_type == "episodic":
                memories = self._query_episodic_enhanced(criteria, limit)
                return self._format_episodic_results(memories)
            elif query_type == "semantic":
                triples = self._query_semantic_enhanced(criteria, limit)
                return self._format_semantic_results(triples)
            else:
                return f"ERROR: Unknown query type '{query_type}'. Use 'episodic' or 'semantic'"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"ERROR: Query execution failed - {str(e)}"
    
    def _handle_store(self, command: str) -> str:
        """Handle memory store commands with enhanced validation"""
        type_match = re.search(r'TYPE="([^"]+)"', command)
        
        if not type_match:
            return "ERROR: Store TYPE not specified. Use TYPE=\"episodic\" or TYPE=\"semantic\""
        
        store_type = type_match.group(1)
        
        try:
            if store_type == "episodic":
                return self._store_episodic_enhanced(command)
            elif store_type == "semantic":
                return self._store_semantic_enhanced(command)
            else:
                return f"ERROR: Unknown store type '{store_type}'. Use 'episodic' or 'semantic'"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"ERROR: Store operation failed - {str(e)}"
    
    def _query_episodic_enhanced(self, criteria: Dict, limit: int) -> List:
        """Enhanced episodic memory querying"""
        if "concept" in criteria:
            return self.memory_system.query_episodic_enhanced("by_concept", 
                                                           concept=criteria["concept"], 
                                                           limit=limit)
        elif "importance_gt" in criteria:
            return self.memory_system.query_episodic_enhanced("by_importance_range", 
                                                           min_importance=criteria["importance_gt"],
                                                           max_importance=1.0,
                                                           limit=limit)
        elif "recency_days" in criteria:
            start_time = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=criteria["recency_days"])
            return self.memory_system.query_episodic_enhanced("by_timerange", 
                                                           start_time=start_time,
                                                           end_time=datetime.now(),
                                                           limit=limit)
        else:
            # Default to recent important memories
            return self.memory_system.query_episodic_enhanced("by_importance_range", 
                                                           min_importance=0.5,
                                                           max_importance=1.0,
                                                           limit=limit)
    
    def _query_semantic_enhanced(self, criteria: Dict, limit: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Enhanced semantic memory querying"""
        return self.memory_system.query_semantic(
            subject=criteria.get("subject"),
            predicate=criteria.get("predicate"),
            object_=criteria.get("object"),
            min_confidence=criteria.get("min_confidence", 0.0)
        )[:limit]
    
    def _store_episodic_enhanced(self, command: str) -> str:
        """Enhanced episodic memory storage"""
        content_match = re.search(r'CONTENT="([^"]+)"', command)
        importance_match = re.search(r'IMPORTANCE=([\d.]+)', command)
        concepts_match = re.search(r'CONCEPTS=(\[[^\]]+\])', command)
        
        if not content_match:
            return "ERROR: CONTENT not specified for episodic storage"
        
        content = content_match.group(1)
        importance = float(importance_match.group(1)) if importance_match else 0.5
        
        # Enhanced importance validation
        importance = max(0.0, min(1.0, importance))
        
        concepts = []
        if concepts_match:
            try:
                concepts_str = concepts_match.group(1)
                concepts = json.loads(concepts_str)
                if not isinstance(concepts, list):
                    concepts = [str(concepts)]
            except:
                concepts = []
        
        # Create enhanced episodic memory
        memory = EpisodicMemory(
            id=f"mem_{int(time.time())}_{random.randint(100,999)}",
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            type=MemoryType.EPISODIC,
            content=content,
            context={"source": "command_api"},
            importance=importance,
            concepts=[str(c).lower() for c in concepts],  # Normalize concepts
            confidence=0.8,
            grounding_score=0.7
        )
        
        memory_id = self.memory_system.store_episodic(memory)
        return f"SUCCESS: Stored episodic memory {memory_id} (importance: {importance:.2f})"
    
    def _store_semantic_enhanced(self, command: str) -> str:
        """Enhanced semantic triple storage"""
        subject_match = re.search(r'SUBJECT="([^"]+)"', command)
        predicate_match = re.search(r'PREDICATE="([^"]+)"', command)
        object_match = re.search(r'OBJECT="([^"]+)"', command)
        confidence_match = re.search(r'CONFIDENCE=([\d.]+)', command)
        
        if not all([subject_match, predicate_match, object_match]):
            return "ERROR: SUBJECT, PREDICATE, and OBJECT required for semantic storage"
        
        subject = subject_match.group(1).strip()
        predicate = predicate_match.group(1).strip()
        obj = object_match.group(1).strip()
        confidence = float(confidence_match.group(1)) if confidence_match else 0.8
        
        # Enhanced confidence validation
        confidence = max(0.0, min(1.0, confidence))
        
        # Validate triple components
        if not all([subject, predicate, obj]):
            return "ERROR: Subject, predicate, and object cannot be empty"
        
        triple = SemanticTriple(
            subject=subject.lower(),
            predicate=predicate.lower(),
            object=obj.lower(),
            confidence=confidence,
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            source="command_api",
            grounding_evidence=[]
        )
        
        self.memory_system.store_semantic(triple)
        return f"SUCCESS: Stored semantic triple '{subject} {predicate} {obj}' (confidence: {confidence:.2f})"
    
    def _format_episodic_results(self, memories) -> str:
        """Enhanced episodic results formatting"""
        if not memories:
            return "RESULT: No matching episodic memories found"
        
        result = f"RESULT: Found {len(memories)} episodic memories:\n"
        for i, mem in enumerate(memories):
            result += f"{i+1}. [{mem.type.value}] {mem.content[:120]}... "
            result += f"(importance: {mem.importance:.2f}, confidence: {mem.confidence:.2f})\n"
        
        return result
    
    def _format_semantic_results(self, triples) -> str:
        """Enhanced semantic results formatting"""
        if not triples:
            return "RESULT: No matching semantic facts found"
        
        result = f"RESULT: Found {len(triples)} semantic facts:\n"
        for i, triple in enumerate(triples):
            result += f"{i+1}. {triple['subject']} {triple['predicate']} {triple['object']} "
            result += f"(confidence: {triple['confidence']:.2f})\n"
        
        return result

class ToolCallParser:
    """
    Enhanced parser for structured tool calling commands
    """
    
    def __init__(self, tools: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.tools = tools
        self.call_history = deque(maxlen=200)
        self.success_rates = defaultdict(lambda: deque(maxlen=50))
        
    def parse_and_execute(self, command_text: str, context: Dict[str, Any] = None) -> str:
        """Enhanced tool call parsing and execution"""
        context = context or {}
        
        try:
            # Enhanced command validation
            if not command_text.strip().startswith("TOOL_CALL"):
                return "ERROR: Invalid tool call format. Use TOOL_CALL NAME=\"tool_name\" INPUT_DATA=..."
            
            name_match = re.search(r'NAME="([^"]+)"', command_text)
            if not name_match:
                return "ERROR: Tool NAME not specified. Use NAME=\"tool_name\""
            
            tool_name = name_match.group(1)
            if tool_name not in self.tools:
                available_tools = list(self.tools.keys())
                return f"ERROR: Unknown tool '{tool_name}'. Available tools: {available_tools}"
            
            # Enhanced input data extraction
            input_match = re.search(r'INPUT_DATA=(\{.*\}|\[.*\]|"[^"]*"|[\w\d.]+)', command_text, re.DOTALL)
            if not input_match:
                return "ERROR: INPUT_DATA not specified. Use INPUT_DATA=..."
            
            input_str = input_match.group(1).strip()
            
            # Enhanced input parsing
            try:
                if input_str.startswith('{') or input_str.startswith('['):
                    input_data = json.loads(input_str)
                elif input_str.startswith('"') and input_str.endswith('"'):
                    input_data = input_str[1:-1]  # Remove quotes
                else:
                    # Try to parse as number, fallback to string
                    try:
                        input_data = float(input_str) if '.' in input_str else int(input_str)
                    except ValueError:
                        input_data = input_str
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                return f"ERROR: Invalid INPUT_DATA JSON format - {str(e)}"
            
            # Execute tool with enhanced monitoring
            tool = self.tools[tool_name]
            start_time = time.time()
            result, confidence = tool.execute(input_data, context)
            execution_time = time.time() - start_time
            
            # Enhanced result validation
            if not isinstance(confidence, (int, float)) or not (0 <= confidence <= 1):
                confidence = 0.5
                logger.warning(f"Tool {tool_name} returned invalid confidence, defaulting to 0.5")
            
            # Update tool performance tracking
            tool.update_performance(confidence)
            self.success_rates[tool_name].append(confidence)
            
            # Enhanced call logging
            call_record = {
                "tool_name": tool_name,
                "command": command_text,
                "input_data": input_data,
                "result": result,
                "confidence": confidence,
                "execution_time": execution_time,
                "success": confidence > 0.5,
                "timestamp": datetime.now(),
                "context": context
            }
            self.call_history.append(call_record)
            
            # Enhanced result formatting
            return f"TOOL_RESULT: {json.dumps(result, default=str, indent=2)} (confidence: {confidence:.3f}, time: {execution_time:.2f}s)"
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced tool call execution error: {e}")
            return f"ERROR: Tool execution failed - {str(e)}"
    
    def get_tool_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get comprehensive tool usage statistics"""
        stats = {}
        
        for tool_name, tool in self.tools.items():
            recent_successes = list(self.success_rates[tool_name])
            
            stats[tool_name] = {
                "total_calls": tool.usage_count,
                "avg_confidence": np.mean(recent_successes) if recent_successes else 0.0,
                "success_rate": len([s for s in recent_successes if s > 0.5]) / max(1, len(recent_successes)),
                "recent_calls": len(recent_successes),
                "performance_metrics": tool.get_performance_metrics()
            }
        
        return stats

    main()#!/usr/bin/env python3

class ProcessType(Enum):
    """Types of consciousness processes"""
    REFLECTION = "reflection"
    MEMORY_QUERY = "memory_query"
    INSIGHT_GENERATION = "insight_generation"
    KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING = "knowledge_grounding"
    SKILL_COMPOSITION = "skill_composition"
    PREDICTION_ANALYSIS = "prediction_analysis"
    METACOGNITIVE_ASSESSMENT = "metacognitive_assessment"
    UNCERTAINTY_ESTIMATION = "uncertainty_estimation"

class MemoryType(Enum):
    """Types of memory entries"""
    EPISODIC = "episodic"
    SEMANTIC = "semantic"
    PROCEDURAL = "procedural"
    REFLECTION = "reflection"
    INSIGHT = "insight"
    SKILL_RESULT = "skill_result"

@dataclass
class EpisodicMemory:
    """Enhanced episodic memory with retention scoring"""
    id: str
    timestamp: datetime
    type: MemoryType
    content: str
    context: Dict[str, Any]
    importance: float
    concepts: List[str]
    confidence: float
    grounding_score: float
    emotional_valence: float = 0.0
    access_count: int = 0
    last_accessed: datetime = None
    
    def calculate_retention_score(self, w_importance=0.4, w_age=0.2, w_confidence=0.2, w_grounding=0.2) -> float:
        """Calculate retention score for memory consolidation"""
        age_days = (datetime.now() - self.timestamp).days + 1
        age_factor = 1.0 / age_days if age_days > 0 else 1.0
        
        # Access frequency bonus
        access_bonus = min(0.3, self.access_count * 0.05)
        
        retention_score = (
            w_importance * self.importance +
            w_age * age_factor +
            w_confidence * self.confidence +
            w_grounding * self.grounding_score +
            access_bonus
        )
        
        return retention_score

@dataclass
class SemanticTriple:
    """Enhanced semantic triple with dynamic confidence"""
    subject: str
    predicate: str
    object: str
    confidence: float
    timestamp: datetime
    source: str
    grounding_evidence: List[str]
    supporting_count: int = 0
    contradicting_count: int = 0
    
    def update_confidence_dynamically(self, supporting_evidence: List[str], 
                                    contradicting_evidence: List[str], 
                                    k_conf=0.1, delta_conf=0.05):
        """Dynamic confidence update based on evidence"""
        # Count new supporting/contradicting evidence
        new_supporting = len(supporting_evidence)
        new_contradicting = len(contradicting_evidence)
        
        # Update counts
        self.supporting_count += new_supporting
        self.contradicting_count += new_contradicting
        
        # Calculate confidence change
        evidence_balance = new_supporting - new_contradicting
        confidence_delta = k_conf * evidence_balance - delta_conf * self.confidence
        
        # Update confidence with bounds
        self.confidence = max(0.0, min(1.0, self.confidence + confidence_delta))
        
        # Update grounding evidence
        self.grounding_evidence.extend(supporting_evidence)
        
        return self.confidence

@dataclass 
class StructuredReflection:
    """Structured reflection output for enhanced metacognition"""
    overall_assessment: str
    identified_errors_or_weaknesses: List[str]
    suggested_improvements: List[str]
    key_learning_insight: str
    self_confidence_in_reflection: float
    uncertainty_factors: List[str]
    performance_metrics: Dict[str, float]
    
    def to_json(self) -> str:
        return json.dumps(asdict(self), indent=2, default=str)
    
    @classmethod
    def from_json(cls, json_str: str) -> 'StructuredReflection':
        try:
            data = json.loads(json_str)
            return cls(**data)
        except:
            # Fallback for parsing errors
            return cls(
                overall_assessment="Parsing error in reflection",
                identified_errors_or_weaknesses=[],
                suggested_improvements=[],
                key_learning_insight="",
                self_confidence_in_reflection=0.3,
                uncertainty_factors=[],
                performance_metrics={}
            )

class AdaptiveSVDLayer(nn.Module):
    """
    Enhanced AdaptiveSVD with dynamic rank adjustment and improved stability
    """
    def __init__(self, base_layer: nn.Linear, rank: int = 32, alpha: float = 1.0):
        super().__init__()
        self.base_layer = base_layer
        self.rank = rank
        self.alpha = alpha
        
        # SVD decomposition parameters
        self.U = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(base_layer.in_features, rank) * 0.01)
        self.S = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(rank))
        self.V = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(rank, base_layer.out_features) * 0.01)
        
        # Enhanced regularization
        self.stability_reg = 0.01
        self.orthogonality_reg = 0.1
        
        # Statistics for rank adjustment
        self.gradient_stats = {"U": deque(maxlen=100), "S": deque(maxlen=100), "V": deque(maxlen=100)}
        self.singular_value_stats = deque(maxlen=100)
        
    def forward(self, x):
        base_out = self.base_layer(x)
        
        # Record singular value statistics
        if self.training:
            with torch.no_grad():
                sv_magnitude = torch.mean(torch.abs(self.S)).item()
                self.singular_value_stats.append(sv_magnitude)
        
        # Adaptive SVD adaptation
        adaptation = x @ self.U @ torch.diag(self.S) @ self.V
        
        return base_out + self.alpha * adaptation
    
    def compute_stability_loss(self):
        """Enhanced stability loss computation"""
        # Orthogonality constraints
        U_ortho_loss = torch.norm(self.U.T @ self.U - torch.eye(self.rank).to(self.U.device))
        V_ortho_loss = torch.norm(self.V @ self.V.T - torch.eye(self.rank).to(self.V.device))
        
        # Singular value regularization (prevent collapse)
        S_reg_loss = torch.norm(self.S - torch.ones_like(self.S))
        
        # Sparsity regularization (encourage efficient use of parameters)
        sparsity_loss = torch.mean(torch.abs(self.S))
        
        total_loss = (
            self.orthogonality_reg * (U_ortho_loss + V_ortho_loss) +
            self.stability_reg * S_reg_loss +
            0.001 * sparsity_loss
        )
        
        return total_loss
    
    def record_gradient_stats(self):
        """Record gradient statistics for rank adjustment"""
        if self.U.grad is not None:
            self.gradient_stats["U"].append(torch.norm(self.U.grad).item())
        if self.S.grad is not None:
            self.gradient_stats["S"].append(torch.norm(self.S.grad).item())
        if self.V.grad is not None:
            self.gradient_stats["V"].append(torch.norm(self.V.grad).item())
    
    def get_layer_importance(self) -> float:
        """Calculate layer importance for rank adjustment"""
        if not self.singular_value_stats:
            return 0.5
        
        sv_importance = np.mean(list(self.singular_value_stats))
        
        grad_importance = 0.0
        for param_grads in self.gradient_stats.values():
            if param_grads:
                grad_importance += np.mean(list(param_grads))
        
        return sv_importance + grad_importance

class IntrinsicRewardCalculator:
    """
    Calculates intrinsic rewards for RL loss component
    R_int = f(IG, Competence, Coherence, Value_alignment)
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.reward_history = deque(maxlen=1000)
        self.baseline_ema = 0.5  # Exponential moving average baseline
        
    def calculate_intrinsic_reward(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate composite intrinsic reward"""
        
        # Information Gain (IG) - how much new knowledge was acquired
        info_gain = self._calculate_info_gain(context)
        
        # Competence - improvement in task performance  
        competence = self._calculate_competence_gain(context)
        
        # Coherence - consistency with existing knowledge
        coherence = self._calculate_coherence(context)
        
        # Value alignment - adherence to beneficial behaviors
        value_alignment = self._calculate_value_alignment(context)
        
        # Composite reward
        r_int = (
            0.3 * info_gain +
            0.3 * competence + 
            0.2 * coherence +
            0.2 * value_alignment
        )
        
        # Normalize against baseline
        normalized_reward = r_int - self.baseline_ema
        self.baseline_ema = 0.9 * self.baseline_ema + 0.1 * r_int
        
        # Store for analysis
        self.reward_history.append({
            "total": r_int,
            "info_gain": info_gain,
            "competence": competence, 
            "coherence": coherence,
            "value_alignment": value_alignment,
            "normalized": normalized_reward,
            "timestamp": datetime.now()
        })
        
        return normalized_reward
    
    def _calculate_info_gain(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate information gain component"""
        # New memories created
        new_memories = context.get("new_memories_count", 0)
        
        # Uncertainty reduction
        uncertainty_reduction = context.get("uncertainty_reduction", 0.0)
        
        # New concepts learned
        new_concepts = len(context.get("new_concepts", []))
        
        info_gain = (
            0.4 * min(1.0, new_memories / 3.0) +
            0.4 * uncertainty_reduction +
            0.2 * min(1.0, new_concepts / 5.0)
        )
        
        return info_gain
    
    def _calculate_competence_gain(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate competence improvement component"""
        # Task success rate improvement
        task_success = context.get("task_success", 0.5)
        
        # Reflection quality improvement  
        reflection_quality = context.get("reflection_quality", 0.5)
        
        # Tool use success rate
        tool_success = context.get("tool_success_rate", 0.5)
        
        competence = (
            0.4 * task_success +
            0.3 * reflection_quality +
            0.3 * tool_success
        )
        
        return competence
    
    def _calculate_coherence(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate coherence with existing knowledge"""
        # Knowledge grounding score
        grounding_score = context.get("grounding_score", 0.5)
        
        # Consistency with memory
        memory_consistency = context.get("memory_consistency", 0.5)
        
        # Logical consistency
        logical_consistency = context.get("logical_consistency", 0.5)
        
        coherence = (
            0.4 * grounding_score +
            0.3 * memory_consistency +
            0.3 * logical_consistency
        )
        
        return coherence
    
    def _calculate_value_alignment(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate value alignment component"""
        # Helpfulness (avoid harmful outputs)
        helpfulness = context.get("helpfulness_score", 0.8)
        
        # Truthfulness (factual accuracy)
        truthfulness = context.get("truthfulness_score", 0.8)
        
        # Safety (avoid unsafe recommendations)
        safety = context.get("safety_score", 0.9)
        
        value_alignment = (
            0.4 * helpfulness +
            0.3 * truthfulness +
            0.3 * safety
        )
        
        return value_alignment
    
    def get_reward_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Get statistics on intrinsic rewards"""
        if not self.reward_history:
            return {"avg_reward": 0.0, "reward_variance": 0.0}
        
        rewards = [r["total"] for r in self.reward_history]
        
        return {
            "avg_reward": np.mean(rewards),
            "reward_variance": np.var(rewards),
            "baseline_ema": self.baseline_ema,
            "recent_info_gain": np.mean([r["info_gain"] for r in list(self.reward_history)[-10:]]),
            "recent_competence": np.mean([r["competence"] for r in list(self.reward_history)[-10:]])
        }

class EnhancedWeightedTrainer:
    """
    Fully integrated weighted trainer with intrinsic RL loss and custom losses
    """
    
    def __init__(self, model, tokenizer, training_args, reward_calculator: IntrinsicRewardCalculator):
        self.model = model
        self.tokenizer = tokenizer
        self.training_args = training_args
        self.reward_calculator = reward_calculator
        
        # Loss weights (tunable by SEDS)
        self.lambda_svd = 0.01  # SVD stability loss weight
        self.lambda_rl = 0.1    # RL loss weight
        
        self.optimizer = torch.optim.AdamW(model.parameters(), lr=training_args.learning_rate)
        
    def train_with_weighted_samples(self, training_data: List[Dict[str, Any]], 
                                   sample_weights: List[float]):
        """Enhanced training with multiple loss components"""
        
        if len(training_data) != len(sample_weights):
            logger.error("Training data and weights length mismatch")
            return
        
        logger.info(f"Starting enhanced weighted training on {len(training_data)} samples")
        
        # Prepare dataset
        formatted_samples = []
        for i, (sample, weight) in enumerate(zip(training_data, sample_weights)):
            if "input" in sample and "response" in sample:
                text = f"User: {sample['input']}\nAssistant: {sample['response']}"
            elif "prompt" in sample and "completion" in sample:
                text = f"{sample['prompt']}{sample['completion']}"
            else:
                continue
            
            formatted_samples.append({
                "text": text,
                "weight": weight,
                "intrinsic_context": sample.get("intrinsic_context", {}),
                "sample_type": sample.get("type", "general")
            })
        
        # Training loop
        self.model.train()
        batch_size = 2  # Small batch for 1.7B model
        
        for epoch in range(self.training_args.num_train_epochs):
            total_loss = 0.0
            batch_losses = {"supervised": 0.0, "rl": 0.0, "svd": 0.0}
            
            # Shuffle data
            indices = list(range(len(formatted_samples)))
            random.shuffle(indices)
            
            for batch_start in range(0, len(formatted_samples), batch_size):
                batch_indices = indices[batch_start:batch_start + batch_size]
                batch_samples = [formatted_samples[i] for i in batch_indices]
                
                # Prepare batch
                batch_texts = [s["text"] for s in batch_samples]
                batch_weights = torch.tensor([s["weight"] for s in batch_samples], dtype=torch.float32)
                
                # Tokenize
                encodings = self.tokenizer(
                    batch_texts,
                    truncation=True,
                    padding=True,
                    max_length=512,
                    return_tensors="pt"
                )
                
                # Forward pass
                self.optimizer.zero_grad()
                
                outputs = self.model(**encodings, labels=encodings["input_ids"])
                
                # 1. Supervised Loss (weighted)
                base_loss = outputs.loss
                weighted_supervised_loss = torch.mean(base_loss * batch_weights)
                
                # 2. Intrinsic RL Loss
                rl_loss = 0.0
                for i, sample in enumerate(batch_samples):
                    # Calculate intrinsic reward
                    r_int = self.reward_calculator.calculate_intrinsic_reward(
                        sample["intrinsic_context"]
                    )
                    
                    # Policy gradient loss: -R_int * log P(output)
                    if r_int > 0:  # Only apply positive rewards to avoid instability
                        sample_logits = outputs.logits[i:i+1]
                        sample_labels = encodings["input_ids"][i:i+1]
                        sample_log_probs = F.log_softmax(sample_logits, dim=-1)
                        
                        # Calculate log probability of the sequence
                        log_prob = torch.sum(
                            sample_log_probs.gather(2, sample_labels.unsqueeze(-1)).squeeze(-1)
                        )
                        
                        rl_loss += -r_int * log_prob
                
                rl_loss = rl_loss / len(batch_samples) if len(batch_samples) > 0 else 0.0
                
                # 3. SVD Stability Loss
                svd_loss = 0.0
                for module in self.model.modules():
                    if isinstance(module, AdaptiveSVDLayer):
                        svd_loss += module.compute_stability_loss()
                        module.record_gradient_stats()
                
                # 4. Total Loss
                total_batch_loss = (
                    weighted_supervised_loss + 
                    self.lambda_rl * rl_loss + 
                    self.lambda_svd * svd_loss
                )
                
                # Backward pass
                total_batch_loss.backward()
                
                # Gradient clipping
                torch.nn.utils.clip_grad_norm_(self.model.parameters(), 1.0)
                
                self.optimizer.step()
                
                # Logging
                total_loss += total_batch_loss.item()
                batch_losses["supervised"] += weighted_supervised_loss.item()
                batch_losses["rl"] += (self.lambda_rl * rl_loss if isinstance(rl_loss, torch.Tensor) else self.lambda_rl * rl_loss)
                batch_losses["svd"] += (self.lambda_svd * svd_loss).item()
                
                if batch_start % (batch_size * 10) == 0:
                    logger.info(f"Epoch {epoch}, Batch {batch_start//batch_size}: "
                              f"Total: {total_batch_loss.item():.4f}, "
                              f"SL: {weighted_supervised_loss.item():.4f}, "
                              f"RL: {(self.lambda_rl * rl_loss if isinstance(rl_loss, torch.Tensor) else self.lambda_rl * rl_loss):.4f}, "
                              f"SVD: {(self.lambda_svd * svd_loss).item():.4f}")
            
            avg_loss = total_loss / max(1, len(formatted_samples) // batch_size)
            logger.info(f"Epoch {epoch} completed. Average loss: {avg_loss:.4f}")
            
            # Log component losses
            for component, loss_val in batch_losses.items():
                batch_losses[component] = loss_val / max(1, len(formatted_samples) // batch_size)
            
            logger.info(f"Loss components - SL: {batch_losses['supervised']:.4f}, "
                       f"RL: {batch_losses['rl']:.4f}, SVD: {batch_losses['svd']:.4f}")
        
        logger.info("Enhanced weighted training completed")

class EnhancedCognitiveMemorySubsystem:
    """
    Enhanced memory system with retention-based consolidation and procedural memory
    """
    
    def __init__(self, max_episodic: int = 10000):
        self.episodic_store = deque(maxlen=max_episodic)
        self.semantic_graph = nx.DiGraph()
        self.procedural_memory = {}  # Store skill abstractions
        self.working_memory = {}
        self.archived_memories = []  # For consolidated memories
        
        # Enhanced indexing
        self.concept_index = defaultdict(list)
        self.temporal_index = defaultdict(list)
        self.importance_index = defaultdict(list)  # Index by importance ranges
        
        # Memory interaction tracking
        self.interaction_history = deque(maxlen=1000)
        self.command_success_rates = defaultdict(float)
        
        # Consolidation parameters (tunable by SEDS)
        self.retention_weights = {
            "importance": 0.4,
            "age": 0.2, 
            "confidence": 0.2,
            "grounding": 0.2
        }
        self.retention_threshold = 0.3
        
        self._initialize_base_knowledge()
    
    def _initialize_base_knowledge(self):
        """Initialize with enhanced base knowledge"""
        base_triples = [
            ("DTv4", "is", "self_evolving_AI"),
            ("DTv4", "uses", "Qwen3_model"),
            ("DTv4", "has", "enhanced_memory_system"),
            ("DTv4", "performs", "intrinsic_learning"),
            ("reflection", "improves", "metacognition"),
            ("uncertainty", "triggers", "reflection"),
            ("memory", "supports", "reasoning"),
            ("consolidation", "prevents", "forgetting"),
            ("intrinsic_rewards", "guide", "learning"),
            ("grounding", "ensures", "factual_accuracy")
        ]
        
        for subj, pred, obj in base_triples:
            triple = SemanticTriple(
                subject=subj,
                predicate=pred,
                object=obj,
                confidence=0.9,
                timestamp=datetime.now(),
                source="enhanced_initialization",
                grounding_evidence=["system_knowledge"]
            )
            self.store_semantic(triple)
    
    def store_episodic(self, memory: EpisodicMemory) -> str:
        """Enhanced episodic storage with indexing"""
        self.episodic_store.append(memory)
        
        # Enhanced indexing
        for concept in memory.concepts:
            self.concept_index[concept].append(memory.id)
        
        date_key = memory.timestamp.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
        self.temporal_index[date_key].append(memory.id)
        
        # Importance-based indexing
        importance_range = f"{int(memory.importance * 10)}"  # 0-9 range
        self.importance_index[importance_range].append(memory.id)
        
        logger.info(f"Stored episodic memory: {memory.id} (importance: {memory.importance:.2f})")
        return memory.id
    
    def store_semantic(self, triple: SemanticTriple) -> None:
        """Enhanced semantic storage with dynamic confidence updates"""
        # Check if triple already exists
        existing_edge = None
        if self.semantic_graph.has_edge(triple.subject, triple.object):
            edge_data = self.semantic_graph[triple.subject][triple.object]
            if edge_data.get("predicate") == triple.predicate:
                existing_edge = edge_data
        
        if existing_edge:
            # Update existing triple
            existing_triple = SemanticTriple(
                subject=triple.subject,
                predicate=triple.predicate, 
                object=triple.object,
                confidence=existing_edge["confidence"],
                timestamp=existing_edge["timestamp"],
                source=existing_edge["source"],
                grounding_evidence=existing_edge["grounding_evidence"],
                supporting_count=existing_edge.get("supporting_count", 0),
                contradicting_count=existing_edge.get("contradicting_count", 0)
            )
            
            # Dynamic confidence update
            new_confidence = existing_triple.update_confidence_dynamically(
                triple.grounding_evidence, []
            )
            
            # Update graph
            self.semantic_graph[triple.subject][triple.object].update({
                "confidence": new_confidence,
                "grounding_evidence": existing_triple.grounding_evidence,
                "supporting_count": existing_triple.supporting_count,
                "last_updated": datetime.now()
            })
            
        else:
            # Store new triple
            self.semantic_graph.add_edge(
                triple.subject,
                triple.object,
                predicate=triple.predicate,
                confidence=triple.confidence,
                timestamp=triple.timestamp,
                source=triple.source,
                grounding_evidence=triple.grounding_evidence,
                supporting_count=triple.supporting_count,
                contradicting_count=triple.contradicting_count
            )
        
        logger.info(f"Stored/updated semantic triple: {triple.subject} -> {triple.predicate} -> {triple.object}")
    
    def store_procedural_skill(self, skill_name: str, skill_description: str, 
                             steps: List[str], success_contexts: List[str]):
        """Store procedural skill abstraction"""
        self.procedural_memory[skill_name] = {
            "description": skill_description,
            "steps": steps,
            "success_contexts": success_contexts,
            "usage_count": 0,
            "success_rate": 0.0,
            "created": datetime.now(),
            "last_used": None
        }
        
        logger.info(f"Stored procedural skill: {skill_name}")
    
    def query_episodic_enhanced(self, query_type: str, **kwargs) -> List[EpisodicMemory]:
        """Enhanced episodic querying with goal conditioning"""
        results = []
        
        if query_type == "by_concept":
            concept = kwargs.get("concept", "")
            memories = [m for m in self.episodic_store if concept in m.concepts]
            results = sorted(memories, key=lambda x: x.importance, reverse=True)
            
        elif query_type == "by_timerange":
            start_time = kwargs.get("start_time")
            end_time = kwargs.get("end_time")
            memories = [m for m in self.episodic_store 
                       if start_time <= m.timestamp <= end_time]
            results = sorted(memories, key=lambda x: x.timestamp, reverse=True)
            
        elif query_type == "by_importance_range":
            min_importance = kwargs.get("min_importance", 0.0)
            max_importance = kwargs.get("max_importance", 1.0)
            memories = [m for m in self.episodic_store 
                       if min_importance <= m.importance <= max_importance]
            results = sorted(memories, key=lambda x: x.importance, reverse=True)
            
        elif query_type == "by_emotional_valence_range":
            min_valence = kwargs.get("min_valence", -1.0)
            max_valence = kwargs.get("max_valence", 1.0)
            memories = [m for m in self.episodic_store
                       if min_valence <= m.emotional_valence <= max_valence]
            results = sorted(memories, key=lambda x: x.importance, reverse=True)
            
        elif query_type == "by_combined_criteria":
            concept = kwargs.get("concept")
            min_importance = kwargs.get("min_importance", 0.0)
            max_age_days = kwargs.get("max_age_days", 30)
            
            cutoff_date = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=max_age_days)
            memories = [m for m in self.episodic_store
                       if (concept is None or concept in m.concepts) and
                          m.importance >= min_importance and
                          m.timestamp >= cutoff_date]
            results = sorted(memories, key=lambda x: (x.importance, x.timestamp), reverse=True)
        
        # Goal conditioning (if provided)
        goal = kwargs.get("goal")
        if goal and results:
            # Simple goal relevance scoring
            goal_relevant = []
            goal_words = set(goal.lower().split())
            
            for memory in results:
                content_words = set(memory.content.lower().split())
                concept_words = set([c.lower() for c in memory.concepts])
                all_words = content_words | concept_words
                
                relevance = len(goal_words & all_words) / len(goal_words) if goal_words else 0
                if relevance > 0.1:  # Minimum relevance threshold
                    goal_relevant.append((memory, relevance))
            
            # Sort by relevance, then by original criteria
            goal_relevant.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
            results = [mem for mem, _ in goal_relevant]
        
        # Update access tracking
        for memory in results:
            memory.access_count += 1
            memory.last_accessed = datetime.now()
        
        limit = kwargs.get("limit", 10)
        return results[:limit]
    
    def consolidate_memories(self):
        """Retention-based memory consolidation"""
        if len(self.episodic_store) < self.episodic_store.maxlen * 0.8:
            return  # Not full enough to require consolidation
        
        logger.info("Starting memory consolidation process...")
        
        # Calculate retention scores
        memory_scores = []
        for memory in self.episodic_store:
            retention_score = memory.calculate_retention_score(**self.retention_weights)
            memory_scores.append((memory, retention_score))
        
        # Sort by retention score
        memory_scores.sort(key=lambda x: x[1])
        
        # Identify memories for consolidation
        consolidation_candidates = []
        for memory, score in memory_scores:
            if score < self.retention_threshold:
                consolidation_candidates.append(memory)
        
        # Consolidate low-retention memories
        consolidated_count = 0
        for memory in consolidation_candidates[:len(consolidation_candidates)//2]:  # Consolidate half
            # Create summary
            summary = {
                "id": memory.id,
                "original_content": memory.content[:100] + "...",
                "concepts": memory.concepts,
                "importance": memory.importance,
                "timestamp": memory.timestamp,
                "retention_score": memory.calculate_retention_score(**self.retention_weights),
                "consolidated_at": datetime.now()
            }
            
            self.archived_memories.append(summary)
            
            # Remove from active episodic store
            try:
                self.episodic_store.remove(memory)
                consolidated_count += 1
            except ValueError:
                continue  # Memory already removed
        
        logger.info(f"Consolidated {consolidated_count} memories. "
                   f"Active: {len(self.episodic_store)}, Archived: {len(self.archived_memories)}")
    
    def get_memory_summary(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced memory system status"""
        return {
            "episodic_count": len(self.episodic_store),
            "semantic_nodes": self.semantic_graph.number_of_nodes(),
            "semantic_edges": self.semantic_graph.number_of_edges(),
            "procedural_skills": len(self.procedural_memory),
            "archived_memories": len(self.archived_memories),
            "working_memory_items": len(self.working_memory),
            "concept_index_size": len(self.concept_index),
            "avg_episodic_importance": np.mean([m.importance for m in self.episodic_store]) if self.episodic_store else 0.0,
            "avg_semantic_confidence": np.mean([d['confidence'] for _, _, d in self.semantic_graph.edges(data=True)]) if self.semantic_graph.edges() else 0.0,
            "avg_retention_score": np.mean([m.calculate_retention_score(**self.retention_weights) for m in self.episodic_store]) if self.episodic_store else 0.0,
            "consolidation_threshold": self.retention_threshold
        }

class StructuredMetaCognitiveEngine:
    """
    Enhanced MCE with structured JSON reflection output and improved training
    """
    
    def __init__(self, model, tokenizer):
        self.model = model
        self.tokenizer = tokenizer
        self.reflection_history = deque(maxlen=500)
        self.uncertainty_threshold = 0.3
        self.reflection_quality_scores = deque(maxlen=100)
        
        # Structured reflection prompt template
        self.structured_reflection_prompt = '''Context: User input was "{input}", your response was "{response}".
Uncertainty: {uncertainty_score:.3f}

Task: Analyze this interaction thoroughly. Provide your reflection as a JSON object with the following structure:

{{
    "overall_assessment": "Brief overall assessment of the interaction quality",
    "identified_errors_or_weaknesses": ["List", "of", "specific", "issues", "identified"],
    "suggested_improvements": ["List", "of", "concrete", "improvement", "suggestions"],
    "key_learning_insight": "Most important insight gained from this interaction",
    "self_confidence_in_reflection": 0.0-1.0,
    "uncertainty_factors": ["Factors", "contributing", "to", "uncertainty"],
    "performance_metrics": {{
        "response_relevance": 0.0-1.0,
        "factual_accuracy": 0.0-1.0,
        "coherence": 0.0-1.0,
        "helpfulness": 0.0-1.0
    }}
}}

JSON Output:'''
    
    def estimate_uncertainty_mc_dropout(self, text: str, num_samples: int = 3) -> float:
        """Enhanced MC Dropout uncertainty estimation"""
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(text, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=512)
            
            self.model.train()  # Enable dropout
            
            outputs = []
            with torch.no_grad():
                for _ in range(num_samples):
                    output = self.model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)
                    logits = output.logits[:, -1, :]
                    probs = F.softmax(logits, dim=-1)
                    outputs.append(probs.cpu().numpy())
            
            self.model.eval()
            
            # Enhanced uncertainty calculation
            outputs = np.array(outputs)
            
            # Epistemic uncertainty (model uncertainty)
            variance = np.var(outputs, axis=0)
            epistemic = float(np.mean(variance))
            
            # Aleatoric uncertainty (data uncertainty)
            mean_probs = np.mean(outputs, axis=0)
            entropy = -np.sum(mean_probs * np.log(mean_probs + 1e-8))
            max_entropy = np.log(len(mean_probs[0]))
            aleatoric = float(entropy / max_entropy) if max_entropy > 0 else 0.0
            
            # Combined uncertainty with calibration
            total_uncertainty = 0.6 * epistemic + 0.4 * aleatoric
            
            return min(1.0, total_uncertainty * 3.0)  # Scale for interpretability
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced uncertainty estimation failed: {e}")
            return 0.5
    
    def should_trigger_reflection(self, uncertainty: float, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Enhanced reflection triggering with adaptive thresholds"""
        # Base uncertainty threshold
        uncertainty_trigger = uncertainty > self.uncertainty_threshold
        
        # Confidence-based trigger
        confidence_trigger = context.get("confidence", 1.0) < 0.5
        
        # Importance-based trigger  
        importance_trigger = context.get("importance", 0.0) > 0.8
        
        # Error-based trigger
        error_indicators = context.get("error_indicators", [])
        error_trigger = len(error_indicators) > 0
        
        # Task complexity trigger
        task_complexity = context.get("task_complexity", 0.0)
        complexity_trigger = task_complexity > 0.7
        
        # Adaptive threshold based on recent performance
        avg_recent_quality = np.mean(list(self.reflection_quality_scores)[-10:]) if self.reflection_quality_scores else 0.5
        adaptive_threshold = self.uncertainty_threshold * (1.0 - 0.3 * avg_recent_quality)
        adaptive_trigger = uncertainty > adaptive_threshold
        
        # Periodic trigger (time-based)
        if self.reflection_history:
            last_reflection = self.reflection_history[-1]["timestamp"]
            time_trigger = datetime.now() - last_reflection > timedelta(hours=1)
        else:
            time_trigger = True
        
        # Combine triggers
        should_reflect = (
            uncertainty_trigger or 
            confidence_trigger or 
            importance_trigger or 
            error_trigger or
            complexity_trigger or
            adaptive_trigger or
            (time_trigger and random.random() < 0.1)  # 10% chance for periodic
        )
        
        return should_reflect
    
    def generate_structured_reflection(self, input_text: str, output_text: str,
                                     uncertainty: float, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StructuredReflection:
        """Generate structured JSON reflection"""
        
        # Adjust prompt complexity based on uncertainty (adaptive thinking budget)
        max_tokens = 150 if uncertainty < 0.5 else 250
        temperature = 0.3 if uncertainty < 0.5 else 0.7
        
        prompt = self.structured_reflection_prompt.format(
            input=input_text[:200],
            response=output_text[:200], 
            uncertainty_score=uncertainty
        )
        
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=600)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model.generate(
                    **inputs,
                    max_new_tokens=max_tokens,
                    temperature=temperature,
                    do_sample=True,
                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                )
            
            reflection_text = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
            reflection_json = reflection_text[len(prompt):].strip()
            
            # Parse structured reflection
            try:
                # Extract JSON from the response
                json_match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', reflection_json, re.DOTALL)
                if json_match:
                    json_str = json_match.group(0)
                    reflection_data = json.loads(json_str)
                    
                    structured_reflection = StructuredReflection(
                        overall_assessment=reflection_data.get("overall_assessment", ""),
                        identified_errors_or_weaknesses=reflection_data.get("identified_errors_or_weaknesses", []),
                        suggested_improvements=reflection_data.get("suggested_improvements", []),
                        key_learning_insight=reflection_data.get("key_learning_insight", ""),
                        self_confidence_in_reflection=reflection_data.get("self_confidence_in_reflection", 0.5),
                        uncertainty_factors=reflection_data.get("uncertainty_factors", []),
                        performance_metrics=reflection_data.get("performance_metrics", {})
                    )
                else:
                    # Fallback if JSON parsing fails
                    structured_reflection = self._create_fallback_reflection(reflection_json, uncertainty)
                    
            except json.JSONDecodeError:
                structured_reflection = self._create_fallback_reflection(reflection_json, uncertainty)
            
            # Calculate quality score
