            quality_score = self._assess_reflection_quality(structured_reflection)
            
            # Store reflection
            reflection_record = {
                "timestamp": datetime.now(),
                "input_text": input_text,
                "output_text": output_text,
                "uncertainty": uncertainty,
                "context": context,
                "structured_reflection": structured_reflection,
                "quality_score": quality_score,
                "reflection_type": "structured"
            }
            
            self.reflection_history.append(reflection_record)
            self.reflection_quality_scores.append(quality_score)
            
            return structured_reflection
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Structured reflection generation failed: {e}")
            return self._create_fallback_reflection("Generation failed", uncertainty)
    
    def _create_fallback_reflection(self, text: str, uncertainty: float) -> StructuredReflection:
        """Create fallback structured reflection"""
        return StructuredReflection(
            overall_assessment=f"Basic assessment based on text analysis. Uncertainty: {uncertainty:.2f}",
            identified_errors_or_weaknesses=["JSON parsing failed", "Limited reflection capability"],
            suggested_improvements=["Improve structured output", "Enhance reflection training"],
            key_learning_insight="Need better structured reflection capabilities",
            self_confidence_in_reflection=0.3,
            uncertainty_factors=["High uncertainty", "Parsing difficulties"],
            performance_metrics={
                "response_relevance": 0.5,
                "factual_accuracy": 0.5,
                "coherence": 0.4,
                "helpfulness": 0.5
            }
        )
    
    def _assess_reflection_quality(self, reflection: StructuredReflection) -> float:
        """Assess quality of structured reflection"""
        quality_score = 0.0
        
        # Completeness (30%)
        completeness = 0.0
        if reflection.overall_assessment: completeness += 0.2
        if reflection.identified_errors_or_weaknesses: completeness += 0.2
        if reflection.suggested_improvements: completeness += 0.2
        if reflection.key_learning_insight: completeness += 0.2
        if reflection.performance_metrics: completeness += 0.2
        quality_score += 0.3 * completeness
        
        # Depth and specificity (25%)
        depth = 0.0
        depth += min(0.4, len(reflection.identified_errors_or_weaknesses) * 0.1)
        depth += min(0.4, len(reflection.suggested_improvements) * 0.1)
        depth += 0.2 if len(reflection.key_learning_insight) > 20 else 0.0
        quality_score += 0.25 * depth
        
        # Self-awareness (20%)
        self_awareness = reflection.self_confidence_in_reflection
        quality_score += 0.2 * self_awareness
        
        # Performance metrics validity (25%)
        perf_metrics = reflection.performance_metrics
        if perf_metrics:
            valid_metrics = sum(1 for v in perf_metrics.values() if isinstance(v, (int, float)) and 0 <= v <= 1)
            metrics_quality = valid_metrics / max(1, len(perf_metrics))
            quality_score += 0.25 * metrics_quality
        
        return min(1.0, quality_score)
    
    def get_reflection_training_data(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Get enhanced training data for reflection capability"""
        training_data = []
        
        for reflection_record in self.reflection_history:
            if reflection_record.get("quality_score", 0) > 0.6:
                structured_refl = reflection_record["structured_reflection"]
                
                training_data.append({
                    "prompt": self.structured_reflection_prompt.format(
                        input=reflection_record["input_text"][:200],
                        response=reflection_record["output_text"][:200],
                        uncertainty_score=reflection_record["uncertainty"]
                    ),
                    "completion": structured_refl.to_json(),
                    "quality_score": reflection_record["quality_score"],
                    "type": "structured_reflection",
                    "intrinsic_context": {
                        "reflection_quality": reflection_record["quality_score"],
                        "uncertainty_reduction": reflection_record["uncertainty"],
                        "new_concepts": list(set(reflection_record["context"].get("concepts", []))),
                        "helpfulness_score": structured_refl.performance_metrics.get("helpfulness", 0.8),
                        "truthfulness_score": structured_refl.performance_metrics.get("factual_accuracy", 0.8)
                    }
                })
        
        return training_data
    
    def get_metacognitive_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced metacognitive system status"""
        avg_reflection_quality = np.mean(self.reflection_quality_scores) if self.reflection_quality_scores else 0.0
        
        # Calculate structured reflection success rate
        structured_reflections = [r for r in self.reflection_history if r.get("reflection_type") == "structured"]
        structured_success_rate = len(structured_reflections) / max(1, len(self.reflection_history))
        
        return {
            "total_reflections": len(self.reflection_history),
            "structured_reflections": len(structured_reflections),
            "structured_success_rate": structured_success_rate,
            "avg_reflection_quality": float(avg_reflection_quality),
            "uncertainty_threshold": self.uncertainty_threshold,
            "recent_reflections": len([r for r in self.reflection_history 
                                     if datetime.now() - r["timestamp"] < timedelta(hours=24)]),
            "training_data_available": len(self.get_reflection_training_data()),
            "avg_self_confidence": np.mean([
                r["structured_reflection"].self_confidence_in_reflection 
                for r in structured_reflections
            ]) if structured_reflections else 0.0
        }

class NLIEnhancedKnowledgeGrounding:
    """
    Enhanced knowledge grounding with NLI-based support/contradiction detection
    """
    
    def __init__(self, memory_system, model, tokenizer):
        self.memory_system = memory_system
        self.model = model
        self.tokenizer = tokenizer
        self.grounding_cache = {}
        self.fact_verification_history = deque(maxlen=1000)
        
        # NLI prompt template
        self.nli_prompt = '''Task: Determine the logical relationship between two statements.

Statement 1: {statement1}
Statement 2: {statement2}

Choose one:
- ENTAILS: Statement 1 logically supports or implies Statement 2
- CONTRADICTS: Statement 1 contradicts or opposes Statement 2  
- NEUTRAL: No clear logical relationship

Relationship: '''
    
    # Try to load sentence transformer
        try:
            import sentence_transformers
            self.sentence_model = sentence_transformers.SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')
            logger.info("Loaded sentence transformer for enhanced similarity")
        except ImportError:
            self.sentence_model = None
            logger.info("Sentence transformers not available, using SLM-based similarity")
    
    def classify_nli_relationship(self, statement1: str, statement2: str) -> str:
        """Use SLM for NLI classification"""
        prompt = self.nli_prompt.format(statement1=statement1, statement2=statement2)
        
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=400)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model.generate(
                    **inputs,
                    max_new_tokens=10,
                    temperature=0.1,
                    do_sample=True,
                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                )
            
            result = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
            result = result[len(prompt):].strip().upper()
            
            # Extract relationship
            if "ENTAILS" in result:
                return "ENTAILS"
            elif "CONTRADICTS" in result:
                return "CONTRADICTS"
            else:
                return "NEUTRAL"
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"NLI classification failed: {e}")
            return "NEUTRAL"
    
    def extract_concepts_enhanced(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        """Enhanced SLM-based concept extraction with fallback"""
        prompt = f"""Extract the key entities, concepts, and topics (up to 7) from the following text. Focus on nouns, important verbs, and domain-specific terms. Output as a comma-separated list:

Text: {text[:400]}
Key concepts: """
        
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=512)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model.generate(
                    **inputs,
                    max_new_tokens=60,
                    temperature=0.2,
                    do_sample=True,
                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                )
            
            concepts_text = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
            concepts_text = concepts_text[len(prompt):].strip()
            
            # Parse and clean concepts
            concepts = []
            for concept in concepts_text.split(','):
                concept = concept.strip().lower()
                if concept and len(concept) > 2 and len(concept) < 30:
                    concepts.append(concept)
            
            return concepts[:7]
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced concept extraction failed: {e}")
            return self._extract_concepts_fallback(text)
    
    def _extract_concepts_fallback(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        """Fallback concept extraction using NLP patterns"""
        import re
        
        # Extract potential concepts using patterns
        words = re.findall(r'\b[A-Za-z]{3,20}\b', text.lower())
        
        # Filter stopwords and common words
        stopwords = {
            'the', 'and', 'but', 'for', 'are', 'with', 'you', 'that', 'this', 
            'can', 'will', 'have', 'from', 'they', 'been', 'were', 'said', 
            'what', 'make', 'like', 'time', 'very', 'when', 'much', 'would',
            'there', 'each', 'which', 'their', 'than', 'many', 'some', 'these'
        }
        
        concepts = []
        for word in words:
            if word not in stopwords and len(word) > 3:
                concepts.append(word)
        
        # Remove duplicates and limit
        return list(dict.fromkeys(concepts))[:7]
    
    def calculate_enhanced_similarity(self, text1: str, text2: str) -> float:
        """Enhanced semantic similarity calculation"""
        if self.sentence_model:
            try:
                embeddings = self.sentence_model.encode([text1, text2])
                similarity = np.dot(embeddings[0], embeddings[1]) / (
                    np.linalg.norm(embeddings[0]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[1])
                )
                return float(max(0.0, similarity))
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Sentence transformer similarity failed: {e}")
        
        # Fallback to enhanced word overlap
        words1 = set(text1.lower().split())
        words2 = set(text2.lower().split())
        
        if not words1 or not words2:
            return 0.0
        
        # Jaccard similarity
        intersection = len(words1 & words2)
        union = len(words1 | words2)
        jaccard = intersection / union if union > 0 else 0.0
        
        # Weighted overlap (giving more weight to longer words)
        weighted_intersection = sum(len(word) for word in words1 & words2)
        weighted_union = sum(len(word) for word in words1 | words2)
        weighted_overlap = weighted_intersection / weighted_union if weighted_union > 0 else 0.0
        
        # Combined similarity
        return 0.6 * jaccard + 0.4 * weighted_overlap
    
    def ground_statement_with_nli(self, statement: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced grounding with NLI-based evidence evaluation"""
        # Extract concepts
        concepts = self.extract_concepts_enhanced(statement)
        
        # Retrieve relevant facts
        relevant_facts = []
        for concept in concepts[:3]:
            facts = self.memory_system.query_semantic(subject=concept, min_confidence=0.3)
            facts.extend(self.memory_system.query_semantic(object_=concept, min_confidence=0.3))
            relevant_facts.extend(facts[:3])  # Limit per concept
        
        # Remove duplicates
        unique_facts = []
        seen_facts = set()
        for fact in relevant_facts:
            fact_key = (fact['subject'], fact['predicate'], fact['object'])
            if fact_key not in seen_facts:
                unique_facts.append(fact)
                seen_facts.add(fact_key)
        
        # NLI-based evidence classification
        supporting_evidence = []
        contradicting_evidence = []
        neutral_evidence = []
        
        for fact in unique_facts[:8]:  # Limit for performance
            fact_text = f"{fact['subject']} {fact['predicate']} {fact['object']}"
            
            # Skip very similar facts to avoid redundancy
            similarity = self.calculate_enhanced_similarity(statement, fact_text)
            if similarity < 0.2:
                continue
            
            # Classify relationship using NLI
            relationship = self.classify_nli_relationship(statement, fact_text)
            
            fact_with_score = {**fact, 'similarity': similarity, 'nli_relationship': relationship}
            
            if relationship == "ENTAILS":
                supporting_evidence.append(fact_with_score)
            elif relationship == "CONTRADICTS":
                contradicting_evidence.append(fact_with_score)
            else:
                neutral_evidence.append(fact_with_score)
        
        # Calculate enhanced grounding score
        support_score = sum(
            e['confidence'] * e['similarity'] * 1.5  # Boost for entailment
            for e in supporting_evidence
        )
        
        contradiction_penalty = sum(
            e['confidence'] * e['similarity'] * 2.0  # Strong penalty for contradiction
            for e in contradicting_evidence
        )
        
        neutral_contribution = sum(
            e['confidence'] * e['similarity'] * 0.3  # Small contribution for neutral
            for e in neutral_evidence
        ) 
        
        # Confidence-weighted grounding score
        grounding_score = max(0.0, min(1.0, 
            support_score + neutral_contribution - contradiction_penalty
        ))
        
        # Boost score if multiple supporting facts agree
        if len(supporting_evidence) > 1:
            consensus_bonus = min(0.2, (len(supporting_evidence) - 1) * 0.1)
            grounding_score = min(1.0, grounding_score + consensus_bonus)
        
        result = {
            "statement": statement,
            "grounding_score": grounding_score,
            "supporting_evidence": supporting_evidence[:3],
            "contradicting_evidence": contradicting_evidence[:2],
            "neutral_evidence": neutral_evidence[:2],
            "concepts": concepts,
            "nli_classifications": {
                "supporting": len(supporting_evidence),
                "contradicting": len(contradicting_evidence), 
                "neutral": len(neutral_evidence)
            },
            "timestamp": datetime.now(),
            "is_grounded": grounding_score > 0.5
        }
        
        # Cache result
        cache_key = hash(statement)
        self.grounding_cache[cache_key] = result
        
        # Track verification
        self.fact_verification_history.append({
            "statement": statement,
            "grounding_score": grounding_score,
            "evidence_count": len(supporting_evidence) + len(contradicting_evidence),
            "timestamp": datetime.now()
        })
        
        return result
    
    def create_cot_grounded_prompt(self, user_input: str, base_prompt: str, max_steps: int = 3) -> str:
        """Create chain-of-thought grounded prompt with iterative grounding"""
        concepts = self.extract_concepts_enhanced(user_input)
        
        # Get relevant facts for grounding
        relevant_facts = []
        for concept in concepts[:2]:
            facts = self.memory_system.query_semantic(subject=concept, min_confidence=0.6)
            relevant_facts.extend(facts[:2])
        
        if not relevant_facts:
            return base_prompt
        
        # Create fact-enriched prompt
        facts_text = "Relevant verified facts:\n"
        for i, fact in enumerate(relevant_facts[:4]):
            facts_text += f"{i+1}. {fact['subject']} {fact['predicate']} {fact['object']} (confidence: {fact['confidence']:.2f})\n"
        
        cot_prompt = f"""{facts_text}

Based on these facts, let's think through this step by step:

{base_prompt}

Step-by-step reasoning:"""
        
        return cot_prompt
    
    def get_grounding_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced grounding system status"""
        recent_verifications = [v for v in self.fact_verification_history 
                              if datetime.now() - v["timestamp"] < timedelta(hours=24)]
        
        avg_grounding_score = np.mean([v["grounding_score"] for v in recent_verifications]) if recent_verifications else 0.0
        avg_evidence_count = np.mean([v["evidence_count"] for v in recent_verifications]) if recent_verifications else 0.0
        
        return {
            "total_verifications": len(self.fact_verification_history),
            "recent_verifications": len(recent_verifications),
            "avg_grounding_score": float(avg_grounding_score),
            "avg_evidence_per_verification": float(avg_evidence_count),
            "cache_size": len(self.grounding_cache),
            "high_confidence_rate": len([v for v in recent_verifications if v["grounding_score"] > 0.7]) / max(1, len(recent_verifications)),
            "nli_enabled": True,
            "sentence_model_available": self.sentence_model is not None
        }

class MetaLearningScheduler:
    """
    Enhanced scheduler with learned utility prediction and meta-optimization
    """
    
    def __init__(self, processes: List[ProcessType]):
        self.processes = processes
        
        # Learned components
        self.process_utility_predictor = {}  # Simple utility predictors per process
        self.process_rewards = defaultdict(lambda: deque(maxlen=50))
        self.process_outcomes = defaultdict(lambda: deque(maxlen=50))
        self.system_state_history = deque(maxlen=200)
        
        # Tunable weights (optimized by SEDS)
        self.weights = {
            "uncertainty": 0.25,
            "info_gain": 0.25,
            "utility": 0.25,
            "exploration": 0.15,
            "competence": 0.05,
            "coherence": 0.05
        }
        
        # Meta-learning parameters
        self.learning_rate = 0.01
        self.weight_bounds = (0.0, 1.0)
        
        # Temperature for softmax
        self.temperature = 1.0
        
        # Goal conditioning
        self.current_goals = []
        self.goal_relevance_cache = {}
    
    def select_process_with_learned_utility(self, system_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> ProcessType:
        """Select process using learned utility predictions"""
        priorities = {}
        
        for process in self.processes:
            # Calculate all factors
            uncertainty_factor = self._get_uncertainty_factor(process, system_state)
            info_gain_factor = self._get_learned_info_gain_factor(process, system_state)
            utility_factor = self._get_learned_utility_factor(process, system_state)
            exploration_factor = self._get_exploration_factor(process, system_state)
            competence_factor = self._get_competence_factor(process, system_state)
            coherence_factor = self._get_coherence_factor(process, system_state)
            
            # Goal relevance (if goals are set)
            goal_relevance = self._get_goal_relevance_factor(process, system_state)
            
            # Weighted combination
            priority = (
                self.weights["uncertainty"] * uncertainty_factor +
                self.weights["info_gain"] * info_gain_factor +
                self.weights["utility"] * utility_factor +
                self.weights["exploration"] * exploration_factor +
                self.weights["competence"] * competence_factor +
                self.weights["coherence"] * coherence_factor +
                0.1 * goal_relevance  # Goal relevance bonus
            )
            
            priorities[process] = priority
        
        # Softmax selection with temperature
        process_list = list(priorities.keys())
        priority_values = np.array([priorities[p] for p in process_list])
        
        # Apply temperature scaling
        scaled_priorities = priority_values / self.temperature
        probabilities = F.softmax(torch.tensor(scaled_priorities), dim=0).numpy()
        
        # Select process
        selected_idx = np.random.choice(len(process_list), p=probabilities)
        selected_process = process_list[selected_idx]
        
        # Store system state for learning
        self.system_state_history.append({
            "state": system_state,
            "selected_process": selected_process,
            "priorities": priorities,
            "timestamp": datetime.now()
        })
        
        logger.info(f"Selected process: {selected_process.value} "
                   f"(priority: {priorities[selected_process]:.3f}, "
                   f"temp: {self.temperature:.2f})")
        
        return selected_process
    
    def _get_learned_info_gain_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate learned information gain factor"""
        # Use historical data to predict info gain
        if process in self.process_outcomes:
            recent_outcomes = list(self.process_outcomes[process])[-10:]
            if recent_outcomes:
                # Average epistemic gain from recent runs
                avg_info_gain = np.mean([o.get("epistemic_gain", 0.0) for o in recent_outcomes])
                
                # Adjust based on current system state
                memory_diversity = state.get("memory_diversity", 0.5)
                uncertainty_level = state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5)
                
                # Scale predicted info gain based on context
                context_multiplier = 1.0
                if process == ProcessType.INSIGHT_GENERATION:
                    context_multiplier = memory_diversity * 2.0
                elif process == ProcessType.REFLECTION:
                    context_multiplier = uncertainty_level * 1.5
                elif process == ProcessType.KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING:
                    context_multiplier = uncertainty_level * 1.2
                
                return min(1.0, avg_info_gain * context_multiplier)
        
        # Fallback to heuristic if no historical data
        return self._get_info_gain_factor_heuristic(process, state)
    
    def _get_learned_utility_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate learned utility factor based on historical performance"""
        if process in self.process_rewards:
            recent_rewards = list(self.process_rewards[process])[-15:]
            if recent_rewards:
                # Exponential moving average of recent rewards
                weights = np.exp(np.arange(len(recent_rewards)) * 0.1)
                weighted_avg = np.average(recent_rewards, weights=weights)
                
                # Adjust for consistency (prefer consistent performers)
                reward_std = np.std(recent_rewards) if len(recent_rewards) > 1 else 0.5
                consistency_bonus = max(0.0, 0.2 - reward_std)
                
                return min(1.0, weighted_avg + consistency_bonus)
        
        return 0.5  # Neutral utility for new processes
    
    def _get_uncertainty_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Enhanced uncertainty factor calculation"""
        system_uncertainty = state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5)
        
        # Process-specific uncertainty reduction capabilities
        uncertainty_reduction_power = {
            ProcessType.REFLECTION: 2.0,
            ProcessType.KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING: 1.5,
            ProcessType.MEMORY_QUERY: 1.2,
            ProcessType.METACOGNITIVE_ASSESSMENT: 1.3,
            ProcessType.UNCERTAINTY_ESTIMATION: 1.8,
            ProcessType.INSIGHT_GENERATION: 0.8,
            ProcessType.SKILL_COMPOSITION: 0.9,
            ProcessType.PREDICTION_ANALYSIS: 1.0
        }
        
        return system_uncertainty * uncertainty_reduction_power.get(process, 1.0)
    
    def _get_exploration_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Enhanced exploration factor with adaptive decay"""
        # Time since last run
        last_run_times = [s["timestamp"] for s in self.system_state_history 
                         if s["selected_process"] == process]
        
        if not last_run_times:
            return 1.0  # Maximum exploration for never-run processes
        
        time_since_run = (datetime.now() - max(last_run_times)).total_seconds() / 3600
        
        # Adaptive exploration based on system performance
        recent_performance = np.mean([
            np.mean(list(priorities.values())) 
            for s in list(self.system_state_history)[-10:]
            for priorities in [s["priorities"]]
        ]) if self.system_state_history else 0.5
        
        # Higher exploration when performance is low
        exploration_multiplier = 1.5 - recent_performance
        
        return min(1.0, time_since_run / 12.0 * exploration_multiplier)  # 12-hour cycle
    
    def _get_competence_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate competence gain potential"""
        # Processes that improve system competence
        competence_processes = {
            ProcessType.SKILL_COMPOSITION: 1.0,
            ProcessType.PREDICTION_ANALYSIS: 0.8,
            ProcessType.REFLECTION: 0.9,
            ProcessType.METACOGNITIVE_ASSESSMENT: 0.7
        }
        
        base_competence = competence_processes.get(process, 0.5)
        
        # Adjust based on recent performance trends
        if process in self.process_rewards:
            recent_rewards = list(self.process_rewards[process])[-5:]
            if len(recent_rewards) >= 2:
                trend = recent_rewards[-1] - recent_rewards[0]
                base_competence += trend * 0.5
        
        return max(0.0, min(1.0, base_competence))
    
    def _get_coherence_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate coherence improvement potential"""
        coherence_processes = {
            ProcessType.KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING: 1.0,
            ProcessType.MEMORY_QUERY: 0.8,
            ProcessType.REFLECTION: 0.7,
            ProcessType.METACOGNITIVE_ASSESSMENT: 0.6
        }
        
        base_coherence = coherence_processes.get(process, 0.4)
        
        # Boost if system coherence is currently low
        avg_grounding_score = state.get("avg_grounding_score", 0.5)
        if avg_grounding_score < 0.6:
            base_coherence *= 1.3
        
        return min(1.0, base_coherence)
    
    def _get_goal_relevance_factor(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate goal relevance factor"""
        if not self.current_goals:
            return 0.5  # Neutral if no goals set
        
        # Simple goal-process relevance mapping
        goal_process_relevance = {
            "learning": [ProcessType.REFLECTION, ProcessType.INSIGHT_GENERATION, ProcessType.MEMORY_QUERY],
            "accuracy": [ProcessType.KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING, ProcessType.UNCERTAINTY_ESTIMATION],
            "efficiency": [ProcessType.SKILL_COMPOSITION, ProcessType.PREDICTION_ANALYSIS],
            "self_improvement": [ProcessType.METACOGNITIVE_ASSESSMENT, ProcessType.REFLECTION]
        }
        
        relevance_score = 0.0
        for goal in self.current_goals:
            relevant_processes = goal_process_relevance.get(goal.lower(), [])
            if process in relevant_processes:
                relevance_score += 1.0 / len(relevant_processes)
        
        return min(1.0, relevance_score)
    
    def _get_info_gain_factor_heuristic(self, process: ProcessType, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Fallback heuristic info gain calculation"""
        if process == ProcessType.INSIGHT_GENERATION:
            return state.get("memory_diversity", 0.5) * 1.5
        elif process == ProcessType.PREDICTION_ANALYSIS:
            return 0.8
        elif process == ProcessType.KNOWLEDGE_GROUNDING:
            return state.get("uncertainty_level", 0.5) * 1.2
        else:
            return 0.6
    
    def update_process_performance(self, process: ProcessType, success_score: float, 
                                  outcome_metrics: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Update learned models with process performance"""
        # Store reward
        self.process_rewards[process].append(success_score)
        
        # Store detailed outcome
        outcome_record = {
            "success_score": success_score,
            "epistemic_gain": outcome_metrics.get("epistemic_gain", 0.0),
            "execution_time": outcome_metrics.get("execution_time", 0.0),
            "timestamp": datetime.now(),
            **outcome_metrics
        }
        self.process_outcomes[process].append(outcome_record)
        
        logger.info(f"Updated {process.value}: reward={success_score:.3f}, "
                   f"epistemic_gain={outcome_metrics.get('epistemic_gain', 0.0):.3f}")
    
    def optimize_weights_simple(self, performance_metric: float):
        """Simple weight optimization based on system performance"""
        # Simple gradient-free optimization
        if not hasattr(self, 'last_performance'):
            self.last_performance = performance_metric
            return
        
        performance_delta = performance_metric - self.last_performance
        
        # If performance improved, reinforce recent weight changes
        # If performance declined, reverse recent weight changes
        if hasattr(self, 'last_weight_changes'):
            for weight_name, change in self.last_weight_changes.items():
                if performance_delta > 0:
                    # Performance improved, continue in same direction
                    self.weights[weight_name] += self.learning_rate * change * performance_delta
                else:
                    # Performance declined, reverse direction
                    self.weights[weight_name] -= self.learning_rate * change * abs(performance_delta)
                
                # Ensure bounds
                self.weights[weight_name] = max(self.weight_bounds[0], 
                                              min(self.weight_bounds[1], self.weights[weight_name]))
        
        # Normalize weights to sum to 1
        total_weight = sum(self.weights.values())
        if total_weight > 0:
            for key in self.weights:
                self.weights[key] /= total_weight
        
        self.last_performance = performance_metric
        logger.info(f"Weight optimization: performance_delta={performance_delta:.3f}, "
                   f"weights={dict(self.weights)}")
    
    def set_goals(self, goals: List[str]):
        """Set current system goals for goal-conditioned scheduling"""
        self.current_goals = goals
        self.goal_relevance_cache.clear()
        logger.info(f"Set scheduler goals: {goals}")
    
    def get_scheduling_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enhanced scheduler status"""
        avg_rewards = {}
        for process, rewards in self.process_rewards.items():
            if rewards:
                avg_rewards[process.value] = float(np.mean(list(rewards)))
        
        return {
            "process_avg_rewards": avg_rewards,
            "weights": dict(self.weights),
            "current_goals": self.current_goals,
            "temperature": self.temperature,
            "total_decisions": len(self.system_state_history),
            "learning_rate": self.learning_rate,
            "recent_performance_trend": self._calculate_performance_trend()
        }
    
    def _calculate_performance_trend(self) -> float:
        """Calculate recent performance trend"""
        if len(self.system_state_history) < 5:
            return 0.0
        
        recent_priorities = [
            np.mean(list(s["priorities"].values()))
            for s in list(self.system_state_history)[-10:]
        ]
        
        if len(recent_priorities) < 2:
            return 0.0
        
        # Simple linear trend
        x = np.arange(len(recent_priorities))
        trend = np.polyfit(x, recent_priorities, 1)[0]
        
        return float(trend)

class TargetedDataCurator:
    """
    Enhanced data curator with targeted synthesis and relevance-driven curation
    """
    
    def __init__(self, model, tokenizer, quality_threshold: float = 0.7):
        self.model = model
        self.tokenizer = tokenizer
        self.quality_threshold = quality_threshold
        
        # Enhanced tracking
        self.data_quality_history = deque(maxlen=1000)
        self.novelty_scores = deque(maxlen=1000)
        self.curation_metrics = defaultdict(int)
        self.targeted_synthesis_history = deque(maxlen=500)
        
        # Learning objectives tracking
        self.learning_objectives = {
            "reflection_quality": {"target": 0.8, "current": 0.5, "priority": 1.0},
            "memory_usage": {"target": 0.9, "current": 0.6, "priority": 0.8},
            "tool_success": {"target": 0.85, "current": 0.7, "priority": 0.9},
            "grounding_accuracy": {"target": 0.8, "current": 0.65, "priority": 1.0}
        }
        
        # Enhanced prompts
        self.quality_assessment_prompt = '''Evaluate the quality of this AI interaction on multiple dimensions. Rate each dimension from 1-10:

Input: {input_text}
Response: {response_text}

Evaluate:
1. Relevance: How well does the response address the input?
2. Coherence: Is the response logically structured and clear?
3. Accuracy: Does the response appear factually correct?
4. Helpfulness: How useful is the response to the user?
5. Depth: Does the response show understanding and insight?

Provide ratings as: Relevance=X, Coherence=X, Accuracy=X, Helpfulness=X, Depth=X
Overall Score (1-10): '''
    
    def assess_quality_enhanced(self, interaction: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Enhanced multi-dimensional quality assessment"""
        input_text = interaction.get("input", "")[:200]
        response_text = interaction.get("response", "")[:300]
        
        if len(response_text.strip()) < 10:
            return {"overall": 0.1, "relevance": 0.1, "coherence": 0.1, 
                   "accuracy": 0.1, "helpfulness": 0.1, "depth": 0.1}
        
        prompt = self.quality_assessment_prompt.format(
            input_text=input_text,
            response_text=response_text
        )
        
        try:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=600)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model.generate(
                    **inputs,
                    max_new_tokens=100,
                    temperature=0.1,
                    do_sample=True,
                    pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token_id
                )
            
            result_text = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
            result_text = result_text[len(prompt):].strip()
            
            # Parse ratings
            ratings = self._parse_quality_ratings(result_text)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Enhanced quality assessment failed: {e}")
            ratings = self._assess_quality_heuristic(interaction)
        
        return ratings
    
    def _parse_quality_ratings(self, text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Parse quality ratings from LLM output"""
        ratings = {}
        
        # Extract individual ratings
        import re
        patterns = {
            "relevance": r"relevance[=:]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)",
            "coherence": r"coherence[=:]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)",
            "accuracy": r"accuracy[=:]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)",
            "helpfulness": r"helpfulness[=:]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)",
            "depth": r"depth[=:]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)"
        }
        
        for dimension, pattern in patterns.items():
            match = re.search(pattern, text.lower())
            if match:
                try:
                    score = float(match.group(1))
                    ratings[dimension] = min(10.0, max(1.0, score)) / 10.0
                except ValueError:
                    ratings[dimension] = 0.5
            else:
                ratings[dimension] = 0.5
        
        # Extract overall score
        overall_match = re.search(r"overall[^:]*[=:]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)", text.lower())
        if overall_match:
            try:
                overall_score = float(overall_match.group(1))
                ratings["overall"] = min(10.0, max(1.0, overall_score)) / 10.0
            except ValueError:
                ratings["overall"] = np.mean(list(ratings.values()))
        else:
            ratings["overall"] = np.mean(list(ratings.values()))
        
        return ratings
    
    def _assess_quality_heuristic(self, interaction: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Fallback heuristic quality assessment"""
        response = interaction.get("response", "")
        input_text = interaction.get("input", "")
        
        # Length appropriateness
        length_score = 0.8 if 20 <= len(response) <= 500 else 0.4
        
        # Relevance (word overlap)
        if input_text:
            input_words = set(input_text.lower().split())
            response_words = set(response.lower().split())
            overlap = len(input_words & response_words) / max(len(input_words), 1)
            relevance_score = min(1.0, overlap * 2)
        else:
            relevance_score = 0.5
        
        # Coherence (sentence structure)
        sentences = response.split('.')
        coherence_score = 0.8 if 2 <= len(sentences) <= 8 else 0.5
        
        # Helpfulness (presence of helpful phrases)
        helpful_phrases = ["here's", "you can", "i recommend", "consider", "try", "help"]
        helpfulness_score = 0.7 + min(0.3, sum(1 for phrase in helpful_phrases if phrase in response.lower()) * 0.1)
        
        overall = (length_score + relevance_score + coherence_score + helpfulness_score) / 4
        
        return {
            "overall": overall,
            "relevance": relevance_score,
            "coherence": coherence_score,
            "accuracy": 0.6,  # Conservative default
            "helpfulness": helpfulness_score,
            "depth": length_score * 0.8
        }
    
    def calculate_relevance_to_objectives(self, item: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
        """Calculate relevance to current learning objectives"""
        relevance_score = 0.0
        
        item_type = item.get("type", "general")
        
        # Map item types to learning objectives
        type_objective_mapping = {
            "reflection": "reflection_quality",
            "memory_interaction": "memory_usage", 
            "tool_use": "tool_success",
            "grounded_response": "grounding_accuracy"
        }
        
        primary_objective = type_objective_mapping.get(item_type)
        if primary_objective and primary_objective in self.learning_objectives:
            obj_info = self.learning_objectives[primary_objective]
            
            # Higher relevance if objective is under-performing
            performance_gap = obj_info["target"] - obj_info["current"]
            relevance_score += obj_info["priority"] * max(0.0, performance_gap * 2.0)
        
        # Additional relevance factors
        quality_score = item.get("quality_score", 0.5)
        confidence = item.get("confidence", 0.5)
        
        # Boost relevance for high-quality items addressing weak areas
        if quality_score > 0.7 and relevance_score > 0.5:
            relevance_score *= 1.3
        
        return min(1.0, relevance_score)
    
    def curate_training_data_targeted(self, conversations: List[Dict[str, Any]], 
                                    reflections: List[Dict[str, Any]], 
                                    tool_uses: List[Dict[str, Any]],
                                    learning_objectives: Dict[str, Any] = None) -> Dict[str, List[Dict[str, Any]]]:
        """Enhanced curation with learning objective targeting"""
        
        if learning_objectives:
            self.learning_objectives.update(learning_objectives)
        
        curated_data = {
            "conversations": [],
            "reflections": [],
            "tool_uses": [],
            "targeted_synthesis": []
        }
        
        # Curate conversations with enhanced quality assessment
        for conv in conversations:
            quality_ratings = self.assess_quality_enhanced(conv)
            novelty_score = self.assess_novelty_perplexity(conv.get("response", ""))
            relevance_score = self.calculate_relevance_to_objectives(conv)
            
            # Composite curation score
            curation_score = (
                0.4 * quality_ratings["overall"] +
                0.3 * novelty_score +
                0.3 * relevance_score
            )
            
            if curation_score >= self.quality_threshold:
                curated_data["conversations"].append({
                    **conv,
                    "quality_ratings": quality_ratings,
                    "novelty_score": novelty_score,
                    "relevance_score": relevance_score,
                    "curation_score": curation_score,
                    "curation_timestamp": datetime.now()
                })
                self.curation_metrics["conversations_accepted"] += 1
            else:
                self.curation_metrics["conversations_rejected"] += 1
        
        # Curate reflections with objective targeting
        for refl in reflections:
            base_quality = refl.get("quality_score", 0.0)
            
            # Boost quality for structured reflections
            if isinstance(refl.get("structured_reflection"), dict):
                base_quality *= 1.2
            
            relevance_score = self.calculate_relevance_to_objectives({
                "type": "reflection", 
                **refl
            })
            
            final_quality = base_quality * (1.0 + 0.5 * relevance_score)
            
            if final_quality >= self.quality_threshold:
                curated_data["reflections"].append({
                    **refl,
                    "enhanced_quality_score": final_quality,
                    "relevance_score": relevance_score
                })
                self.curation_metrics["reflections_accepted"] += 1
            else:
                self.curation_metrics["reflections_rejected"] += 1
        
        # Curate tool uses with success focus
        for tool_use in tool_uses:
            success = tool_use.get("success", False)
            confidence = tool_use.get("confidence", 0.5)
            
            if success and confidence >= 0.6:
                relevance_score = self.calculate_relevance_to_objectives({
                    "type": "tool_use",
                    **tool_use
                })
                
                curated_data["tool_uses"].append({
                    **tool_use,
                    "relevance_score": relevance_score
                })
                self.curation_metrics["tool_uses_accepted"] += 1
            else:
                self.curation_metrics["tool_uses_rejected"] += 1
        
        logger.info(f"Targeted curation completed: "
                   f"{len(curated_data['conversations'])} conversations, "
                   f"{len(curated_data['reflections'])} reflections, "
                   f"{len(curated_data['tool_uses'])} tool uses")
        
        return curated_data
    
    def generate_targeted_synthetic_data(self, curated_data: Dict[str, List[Dict[str, Any]]], 
                                       num_samples: int = 50) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Generate synthetic data targeting specific learning objectives"""
        synthetic_samples = []
        
        # Identify learning gaps
        priority_objectives = sorted(
            self.learning_objectives.items(),
            key=lambda x: (x[1]["target"] - x[1]["current"]) * x[1]["priority"],
            reverse=True
        )
        
        for objective_name, obj_info in priority_objectives[:3]:  # Top 3 objectives
            gap_samples = max(5, int(num_samples * 0.3 * obj_info["priority"]))
            
            logger.info(f"Generating {gap_samples} samples for objective: {objective_name}")
            
            if objective_name == "reflection_quality":
                samples = self._generate_reflection_training_samples(curated_data, gap_samples)
            elif objective_name == "memory_usage":
                samples = self._generate_memory_interaction_samples(curated_data, gap_samples)
            elif objective_name == "tool_success": 
                samples = self._generate_tool_usage_samples(curated_data, gap_samples)
            elif objective_name == "grounding_accuracy":
                samples = self._generate_grounded_response_samples(curated_data, gap_samples)
            else:
                continue
            
            synthetic_samples.extend(samples)
        
        # Add general synthetic samples
        general_samples = num_samples - len(synthetic_samples)
        if general_samples > 0:
            general_synthetic = self._generate_general_synthetic_samples(curated_data, general_samples)
            synthetic_samples.extend(general_synthetic)
        
        logger.info(f"Generated {len(synthetic_samples)} targeted synthetic samples")
        return synthetic_samples
    
    def _generate_reflection_training_samples(self, curated_data: Dict, num_samples: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Generate samples specifically for reflection training"""
        samples = []
        good_reflections = [r for r in curated_data.get("reflections", []) 
                          if r.get("quality_score", 0) > 0.7]
        
        if not good_reflections:
            return samples

            base_reflection = random.choice(good_reflections)
            
            # Create variations with different uncertainty levels
            uncertainty_levels = [0.2, 0.5, 0.8]
            uncertainty = random.choice(uncertainty_levels)
            
            prompt = f'''Given a conversation with uncertainty level {uncertainty:.1f}, generate a high-quality structured reflection.

Example high-quality reflection structure:
{base_reflection.get("structured_reflection", "High-quality reflection example")}

Task: Create a similar high-quality reflection for a conversation with uncertainty {uncertainty:.1f}.
Focus on identifying specific improvements and learning insights.

Reflection: '''
            
            try:
                inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt", truncation=True, max_length=512)
                
                with torch.no_grad():
                    outputs = self.model.generate(
                        **inputs,
                        max_new_tokens=200,
                        temperature=0.7,
                        do_sample=True,
                        pad_token_id=self.tokenizer.eos_token
